# Elixir

[![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/h4cc/awesome-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir/stargazers)

# Awesome Elixir [![CI Badge](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/h4cc/awesome-elixir/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg?style=flat)](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir/actions/workflows/ci.yml/badge.svg/stargazers)](https://github.com/h4cc/awesome-elixir) [![Awesome](https://cdn.rawgit.com/sindresorhus/awesome/d7305f38d29fed78fa85652e3a63e154dd8e8829/media/badge.svg)](https://github.com/sindresorhus/awesome)
A curated list of amazingly awesome Elixir libraries, resources, and shiny things inspired by [awesome-php](https://github.com/ziadoz/awesome-php) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ziadoz/awesome-php?style=flat)](https://github.com/ziadoz/awesome-php/stargazers).

If you think a package should be added, please add a :+1: (`:+1:`) at the according issue or create a new one.

There are [other sites with curated lists of elixir packages](#other-awesome-lists) which you can have a look at.

## Actors
*Libraries and tools for working with actors and such.*
* [alf](https://github.com/antonmi/ALF) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antonmi/ALF?style=flat)](https://github.com/antonmi/ALF/stargazers) - Flow-based Application Layer Framework.
* [bpe](https://github.com/spawnproc/bpe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spawnproc/bpe?style=flat)](https://github.com/spawnproc/bpe/stargazers) - Business Process Engine in Erlang. ([Doc](https://bpe.n2o.dev)).
* [pooler](https://github.com/seth/pooler) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/seth/pooler?style=flat)](https://github.com/seth/pooler/stargazers) - An OTP Process Pool Application.
* [poolex](https://github.com/general-CbIC/poolex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/general-CbIC/poolex?style=flat)](https://github.com/general-CbIC/poolex/stargazers) - Pure elixir pool manager.
* [spawn](https://github.com/eigr/spawn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/eigr/spawn?style=flat)](https://github.com/eigr/spawn/stargazers) - Elixir poliglot actors service mesh.

## Algorithms and Data structures
*Libraries and implementations of algorithms and data structures.*

* [aja](https://github.com/sabiwara/aja) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sabiwara/aja?style=flat)](https://github.com/sabiwara/aja/stargazers) - High performance persistent vectors and ordered maps.
* [array](https://github.com/takscape/elixir-array) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/takscape/elixir-array?style=flat)](https://github.com/takscape/elixir-array/stargazers) - An Elixir wrapper library for Erlang's array.
* [aruspex](https://github.com/dkendal/aruspex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dkendal/aruspex?style=flat)](https://github.com/dkendal/aruspex/stargazers) - Aruspex is a configurable constraint solver, written purely in Elixir.
* [bimap](https://github.com/mkaput/elixir-bimap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mkaput/elixir-bimap?style=flat)](https://github.com/mkaput/elixir-bimap/stargazers) - Pure Elixir implementation of [bidirectional maps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bidirectional_map) and multimaps.
* [bitmap](https://github.com/hashd/bitmap-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashd/bitmap-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/hashd/bitmap-elixir/stargazers) - Pure Elixir implementation of [bitmaps](https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bitmap).
* [blocking_queue](https://github.com/joekain/BlockingQueue) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joekain/BlockingQueue?style=flat)](https://github.com/joekain/BlockingQueue/stargazers) - BlockingQueue is a simple queue implemented as a GenServer. It has a fixed maximum length established when it is created.
* [bloomex](https://github.com/gmcabrita/bloomex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gmcabrita/bloomex?style=flat)](https://github.com/gmcabrita/bloomex/stargazers) - A pure Elixir implementation of Scalable Bloom Filters.
* [clope](https://github.com/ayrat555/clope) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ayrat555/clope?style=flat)](https://github.com/ayrat555/clope/stargazers) - Elixir implementation of CLOPE: A Fast and Effective Clustering Algorithm for Transactional Data.
* [Closure Table](https://github.com/florinpatrascu/closure_table) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/florinpatrascu/closure_table?style=flat)](https://github.com/florinpatrascu/closure_table/stargazers) - Closure Table for Elixir - a simple solution for storing and manipulating complex hierarchies. It provides in-memory and Ecto adapters.
* [combination](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-combination) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/seantanly/elixir-combination?style=flat)](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-combination/stargazers) - Elixir library to generate combinations and permutations from Enumerable collection.
* [conrex](https://github.com/NAISorg/conrex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/NAISorg/conrex?style=flat)](https://github.com/NAISorg/conrex/stargazers) - An Elixir implementation of the CONREC algorithm for topographic or isochrone maps.
* [count_buffer](https://github.com/camshaft/count_buffer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camshaft/count_buffer?style=flat)](https://github.com/camshaft/count_buffer/stargazers) - Buffer a large set of counters and flush periodically.
* [cuckoo](https://github.com/gmcabrita/cuckoo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gmcabrita/cuckoo?style=flat)](https://github.com/gmcabrita/cuckoo/stargazers) - A pure Elixir implementation of [Cuckoo Filters](https://www.cs.cmu.edu/%7Edga/papers/cuckoo-conext2014.pdf).
* [cuid](https://github.com/duailibe/cuid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/duailibe/cuid?style=flat)](https://github.com/duailibe/cuid/stargazers) - Collision-resistant ids optimized for horizontal scaling and sequential lookup performance, written in Elixir.
* [data_morph](https://hex.pm/packages/data_morph) - Create Elixir structs from data.
* [dataframe](https://github.com/JordiPolo/dataframe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/JordiPolo/dataframe?style=flat)](https://github.com/JordiPolo/dataframe/stargazers) - Package providing functionality similar to Python's Pandas or R's data.frame().
* [datastructures](https://github.com/meh/elixir-datastructures) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/elixir-datastructures?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/elixir-datastructures/stargazers) - A collection of protocols, implementations and wrappers to work with data structures.
* [def_memo](https://github.com/os6sense/DefMemo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/os6sense/DefMemo?style=flat)](https://github.com/os6sense/DefMemo/stargazers) - A memoization macro (defmemo) for elixir using a genserver backing store.
* [dlist](https://github.com/stocks29/dlist) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stocks29/dlist?style=flat)](https://github.com/stocks29/dlist/stargazers) - Deque implementations in Elixir.
* [eastar](https://github.com/herenowcoder/eastar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/herenowcoder/eastar?style=flat)](https://github.com/herenowcoder/eastar/stargazers) - A* graph pathfinding in pure Elixir.
* [ecto_materialized_path](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_materialized_path) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asiniy/ecto_materialized_path?style=flat)](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_materialized_path/stargazers) - Tree structure, hierarchy and ancestry for the ecto models.
* [ecto_state_machine](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_state_machine) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asiniy/ecto_state_machine?style=flat)](https://github.com/asiniy/ecto_state_machine/stargazers) - Finite state machine pattern implemented on Elixir and  adopted for Ecto.
* [elistrix](https://github.com/tobz/elistrix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tobz/elistrix?style=flat)](https://github.com/tobz/elistrix/stargazers) - A latency / fault tolerance library to help isolate your applications from an uncertain world of slow or failed services.
* [emel](https://github.com/mrdimosthenis/emel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mrdimosthenis/emel?style=flat)](https://github.com/mrdimosthenis/emel/stargazers) - A simple and functional machine learning library written in elixir.
* [erlang-algorithms](https://github.com/aggelgian/erlang-algorithms) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aggelgian/erlang-algorithms?style=flat)](https://github.com/aggelgian/erlang-algorithms/stargazers) - Implementations of popular data structures and algorithms.
* [exconstructor](https://github.com/appcues/exconstructor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/appcues/exconstructor?style=flat)](https://github.com/appcues/exconstructor/stargazers) - An Elixir library for generating struct constructors that handle external data with ease.
* [exfsm](https://github.com/awetzel/exfsm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awetzel/exfsm?style=flat)](https://github.com/awetzel/exfsm/stargazers) - Simple elixir library to define a static FSM.
* [exmatrix](https://github.com/a115/exmatrix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/a115/exmatrix?style=flat)](https://github.com/a115/exmatrix/stargazers) - ExMatrix is a small library for working with matrices, originally developed for testing matrix multiplication in parallel.
* [exor_filter](https://github.com/mpope9/exor_filter) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mpope9/exor_filter?style=flat)](https://github.com/mpope9/exor_filter/stargazers) - Nif for xor_filters.  'Faster and Smaller Than Bloom and Cuckoo Filters'.
* [ezcryptex](https://github.com/stocks29/ezcryptex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stocks29/ezcryptex?style=flat)](https://github.com/stocks29/ezcryptex/stargazers) - Thin layer on top of Cryptex.
* [flow](https://github.com/dashbitco/flow) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dashbitco/flow?style=flat)](https://github.com/dashbitco/flow/stargazers) - Computational parallel flows on top of GenStage.
* [fnv](https://github.com/asaaki/fnv.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asaaki/fnv.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/asaaki/fnv.ex/stargazers) - Pure Elixir implementation of Fowler–Noll–Vo hash functions.
* [fsm](https://github.com/sasa1977/fsm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sasa1977/fsm?style=flat)](https://github.com/sasa1977/fsm/stargazers) - Finite state machine as a functional data structure.
* [fuse](https://github.com/jlouis/fuse) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jlouis/fuse?style=flat)](https://github.com/jlouis/fuse/stargazers) - This application implements a so-called circuit-breaker for Erlang.
* [gen_fsm](https://github.com/pavlos/gen_fsm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pavlos/gen_fsm?style=flat)](https://github.com/pavlos/gen_fsm/stargazers) - A generic finite state-machine - Elixir wrapper around OTP's gen_fsm.
* [graphex](https://github.com/stocks29/graphex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stocks29/graphex?style=flat)](https://github.com/stocks29/graphex/stargazers) - A library for composing and executing task graphs in elixir.
* [graphmath](https://github.com/crertel/graphmath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/crertel/graphmath?style=flat)](https://github.com/crertel/graphmath/stargazers) - An Elixir library for performing 2D and 3D mathematics.
* [hash_ring_ex](https://github.com/reset/hash-ring-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/reset/hash-ring-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/reset/hash-ring-ex/stargazers) - A consistent hash-ring implementation for Elixir.
* [hypex](https://github.com/whitfin/hypex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/hypex?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/hypex/stargazers) - Fast Elixir implementation of HyperLogLog.
* [indifferent](https://github.com/vic/indifferent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/indifferent?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/indifferent/stargazers) - Indifferent access for Elixir maps/list/tuples with custom key conversion.
* [isaac](https://github.com/arianvp/elixir-isaac) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arianvp/elixir-isaac?style=flat)](https://github.com/arianvp/elixir-isaac/stargazers) - Isaac is an elixir module for ISAAC: a fast cryptographic random number generator.
* [jumper](https://github.com/whitfin/jumper) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/jumper?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/jumper/stargazers) - Jump consistent hash implementation in Elixir (without NIFs).
* [key2value](https://github.com/okeuday/key2value) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/okeuday/key2value?style=flat)](https://github.com/okeuday/key2value/stargazers) - Erlang 2-way Set Associative Map.
* [lfsr](https://github.com/pma/lfsr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pma/lfsr?style=flat)](https://github.com/pma/lfsr/stargazers) - Elixir implementation of a binary Galois Linear Feedback Shift Register.
* [loom](https://github.com/asonge/loom) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asonge/loom?style=flat)](https://github.com/asonge/loom/stargazers) - A CRDT library with δ-CRDT support.
* [luhn](https://github.com/ma2gedev/luhn_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ma2gedev/luhn_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ma2gedev/luhn_ex/stargazers) - Luhn algorithm in Elixir.
* [lz4](https://github.com/szktty/erlang-lz4) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/szktty/erlang-lz4?style=flat)](https://github.com/szktty/erlang-lz4/stargazers) - LZ4 bindings for Erlang for fast data compressing.
* [machinery](https://github.com/joaomdmoura/machinery) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joaomdmoura/machinery?style=flat)](https://github.com/joaomdmoura/machinery/stargazers) - A state machine library for structs in general, it integrates with Phoenix out of the box.
* [mason](https://github.com/spacepilots/mason) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spacepilots/mason?style=flat)](https://github.com/spacepilots/mason/stargazers) - Coerce maps into structs. This is helpful e.g. when you interface a REST API and want to create a struct from the response.
* [matrex](https://github.com/versilov/matrex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/versilov/matrex?style=flat)](https://github.com/versilov/matrex/stargazers) - A blazing fast matrix library for Elixir/Erlang with C implementation using CBLAS.
* [merkle_tree](https://github.com/yosriady/merkle_tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yosriady/merkle_tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/yosriady/merkle_tree/stargazers) - A Merkle hash tree implementation in Elixir.
* [minmaxlist](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-minmaxlist) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/seantanly/elixir-minmaxlist?style=flat)](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-minmaxlist/stargazers) - Elixir library extending `Enum.min_by/2`, `Enum.max_by/2` and `Enum.min_max_by/2` to return a list of results instead of just one.
* [mmath](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/mmath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dalmatinerdb/mmath?style=flat)](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/mmath/stargazers) - A library for performing math on number 'arrays' in binaries.
* [monadex](https://github.com/rob-brown/MonadEx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rob-brown/MonadEx?style=flat)](https://github.com/rob-brown/MonadEx/stargazers) - Upgrade your Elixir pipelines with monads.
* [murmur](https://github.com/gmcabrita/murmur) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gmcabrita/murmur?style=flat)](https://github.com/gmcabrita/murmur/stargazers) - A pure Elixir implementation of the non-cryptographic hash Murmur3.
* [nary_tree](https://github.com/medhiwidjaja/nary_tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/medhiwidjaja/nary_tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/medhiwidjaja/nary_tree/stargazers) - An Elixir implementation of generic n-ary tree data structure.
* [natural_sort](https://github.com/DanCouper/natural_sort) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DanCouper/natural_sort?style=flat)](https://github.com/DanCouper/natural_sort/stargazers) - Elixir natural sort implementation for lists of strings.
* [navigation_tree](https://github.com/gutschilla/elixir-navigation-tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gutschilla/elixir-navigation-tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/gutschilla/elixir-navigation-tree/stargazers) - A navigation tree representation with helpers to generate HTML out of it.
* [parallel_stream](https://github.com/beatrichartz/parallel_stream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/beatrichartz/parallel_stream?style=flat)](https://github.com/beatrichartz/parallel_stream/stargazers) - A parallel stream implementation for Elixir.
* [paratize](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-paratize) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/seantanly/elixir-paratize?style=flat)](https://github.com/seantanly/elixir-paratize/stargazers) - Elixir library providing some handy parallel processing (execution) facilities that support configuring number of workers and timeout.
* [parex](https://github.com/StevenJL/parex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/StevenJL/parex?style=flat)](https://github.com/StevenJL/parex/stargazers) - Parallel Execute (Parex) is an Elixir module for executing multiple (slow) processes in parallel.
* [qcomplex](https://github.com/q60/complex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/q60/complex?style=flat)](https://github.com/q60/complex/stargazers) - Elixir library implementing complex numbers and math operations for them.
* [qex](https://github.com/princemaple/elixir-queue) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/princemaple/elixir-queue?style=flat)](https://github.com/princemaple/elixir-queue/stargazers) - Wraps `:queue`, with improved API and `Inspect`, `Collectable` and `Enumerable` protocol implementations.
* [qrational](https://github.com/q60/rational) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/q60/rational?style=flat)](https://github.com/q60/rational/stargazers) - Elixir library implementing rational numbers and math operations for them.
* [ratio](https://github.com/Qqwy/elixir-rational) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Qqwy/elixir-rational?style=flat)](https://github.com/Qqwy/elixir-rational/stargazers) - Adds Rational Numbers and allows them to be used in common arithmetic operations. Also supports conversion between Floats and Rational Numbers.
* [red_black_tree](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/red_black_tree) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SenecaSystems/red_black_tree?style=flat)](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/red_black_tree/stargazers) - Red-Black tree implementation in Elixir.
* [remodel](https://github.com/stavro/remodel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stavro/remodel?style=flat)](https://github.com/stavro/remodel/stargazers) - An Elixir presenter package used to transform map structures.
* [rendezvous](https://github.com/timdeputter/Rendezvous) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/timdeputter/Rendezvous?style=flat)](https://github.com/timdeputter/Rendezvous/stargazers) - Implementation of the Rendezvous or Highest Random Weight (HRW) hashing algorithm in Elixir.
* [rock](https://github.com/ayrat555/rock) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ayrat555/rock?style=flat)](https://github.com/ayrat555/rock/stargazers) - Elixir implementation of ROCK: A Robust Clustering Algorithm for Categorical Attributes.
* [sfmt](https://github.com/jj1bdx/sfmt-erlang/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jj1bdx/sfmt-erlang/?style=flat)](https://github.com/jj1bdx/sfmt-erlang//stargazers) - SIMD-oriented Fast Mersenne Twister (SFMT) for Erlang.
* [simhash](https://github.com/UniversalAvenue/simhash-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/UniversalAvenue/simhash-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/UniversalAvenue/simhash-ex/stargazers) - Simhash implementation using Siphash and N-grams.
* [sleeplocks](https://github.com/whitfin/sleeplocks) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/sleeplocks?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/sleeplocks/stargazers) - BEAM friendly spinlocks for Elixir/Erlang.
* [sorted_set](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/sorted_set) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SenecaSystems/sorted_set?style=flat)](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/sorted_set/stargazers) - Sorted Sets for Elixir.
* [spacesaving](https://github.com/rozap/spacesaving) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rozap/spacesaving?style=flat)](https://github.com/rozap/spacesaving/stargazers) - stream count distinct element estimation using the "space saving" algorithm.
* [structurez](https://github.com/hamiltop/structurez) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hamiltop/structurez?style=flat)](https://github.com/hamiltop/structurez/stargazers) - A playground for data structures in Elixir.
* [supermemo](https://github.com/edubkendo/supermemo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edubkendo/supermemo?style=flat)](https://github.com/edubkendo/supermemo/stargazers) - An Elixir implementation of the [Supermemo 2 algorithm](https://www.supermemo.com/english/ol/sm2.htm).

* [passwordless_auth](https://github.com/madebymany/passwordless_auth) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/madebymany/passwordless_auth?style=flat)](https://github.com/madebymany/passwordless_auth/stargazers) - Simple passwordless login or 2-factor / multi-factor authentication for Elixir.
* [phauxth](https://github.com/riverrun/phauxth) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/riverrun/phauxth?style=flat)](https://github.com/riverrun/phauxth/stargazers) - Authentication library for Phoenix 1.3 and other Plug-based apps.

## Authorization
*Libraries for implementing Authorization handling.*

* [authorize](https://github.com/jfrolich/authorize) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jfrolich/authorize?style=flat)](https://github.com/jfrolich/authorize/stargazers) - Rule based authorization, for advanced authorization rules.
* [bodyguard](https://github.com/schrockwell/bodyguard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/schrockwell/bodyguard?style=flat)](https://github.com/schrockwell/bodyguard/stargazers) - A flexible authorization library for Phoenix applications.
* [canada](https://github.com/jarednorman/canada) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jarednorman/canada?style=flat)](https://github.com/jarednorman/canada/stargazers) - A simple authorization library that provides a friendly interface using declarative permission rules.
* [canary](https://github.com/cpjk/canary) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cpjk/canary?style=flat)](https://github.com/cpjk/canary/stargazers) - An authorization library for Elixir applications that restricts what resources the current user is allowed to access. ([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/canary/api-reference.html)).
* [speakeasy](https://github.com/coryodaniel/speakeasy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coryodaniel/speakeasy?style=flat)](https://github.com/coryodaniel/speakeasy/stargazers) - Middleware based authentication and authorization for Absinthe GraphQL powered by Bodyguard.
* [terminator](https://github.com/MilosMosovsky/terminator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MilosMosovsky/terminator?style=flat)](https://github.com/MilosMosovsky/terminator/stargazers) - Database based authorization (ACL), with custom DSL rules for requiring needed permissions. ([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/terminator/readme.html)).

## Behaviours and Interfaces

* [connection](https://github.com/fishcakez/connection) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fishcakez/connection?style=flat)](https://github.com/fishcakez/connection/stargazers) - Connection behaviour for connection processes. The API is superset of the GenServer API.
* [gen_state_machine](https://github.com/antipax/gen_state_machine) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antipax/gen_state_machine?style=flat)](https://github.com/antipax/gen_state_machine/stargazers) - Elixir wrapper for gen_statem.

## Caching
*Libraries for caching data.*

* [cachex](https://github.com/whitfin/cachex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/cachex?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/cachex/stargazers) - A powerful caching library for Elixir with a wide featureset.
* [con_cache](https://github.com/sasa1977/con_cache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sasa1977/con_cache?style=flat)](https://github.com/sasa1977/con_cache/stargazers) - ConCache is an ETS based key/value storage.
* [elixir_locker](https://github.com/tsharju/elixir_locker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tsharju/elixir_locker?style=flat)](https://github.com/tsharju/elixir_locker/stargazers) - Locker is an Elixir wrapper for the locker Erlang library that provides some useful libraries that should make using locker a bit easier.
* [jc](https://github.com/jr0senblum/jc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jr0senblum/jc?style=flat)](https://github.com/jr0senblum/jc/stargazers) - In-memory, distributable cache with pub/sub, JSON-query and consistency support.
* [lru_cache](https://github.com/arago/lru_cache) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arago/lru_cache?style=flat)](https://github.com/arago/lru_cache/stargazers) - Simple LRU Cache, implemented with ets.
* [memoize](https://github.com/melpon/memoize) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/melpon/memoize?style=flat)](https://github.com/melpon/memoize/stargazers) - A memoization macro that easily cache function.
* [nebulex](https://github.com/cabol/nebulex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cabol/nebulex?style=flat)](https://github.com/cabol/nebulex/stargazers) - A fast, flexible and extensible distributed and local caching library for Elixir.
* [request_cache_plug](https://github.com/MikaAK/request_cache_plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/MikaAK/request_cache_plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/MikaAK/request_cache_plug/stargazers) - Easy to use caching for requests in either Phoenix Controllers or GraphQL resolvers. Bypasses JSON encoding/decoding for a large speedup.
* [stash](https://github.com/whitfin/stash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/stash?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/stash/stargazers) - A straightforward, fast, and user-friendly key/value store.

## Cloud Infrastructure and Management
*Applications, tools and libraries for your own cloud service.*

* [aws](https://github.com/aws-beam/aws-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aws-beam/aws-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/aws-beam/aws-elixir/stargazers) - AWS clients for Elixir.
* [Batteries Included](https://github.com/batteries-included/batteries-included) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/batteries-included/batteries-included?style=flat)](https://github.com/batteries-included/batteries-included/stargazers) - A self hostable platform for automation/UI driven Kubernetes; built in Elixir and Golang the entire UI is built with Phoenix Live View.
* [Bonny](https://github.com/coryodaniel/bonny) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coryodaniel/bonny?style=flat)](https://github.com/coryodaniel/bonny/stargazers) - Kubernetes Operator Development Framework.
* [Cloudi](http://cloudi.org/) - CloudI is for back-end server processing tasks that require soft-realtime transaction.
* [discovery](https://github.com/undeadlabs/discovery) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/undeadlabs/discovery?style=flat)](https://github.com/undeadlabs/discovery/stargazers) - An OTP application for auto-discovering services with Consul.
* [erlcloud](https://github.com/erlcloud/erlcloud) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/erlcloud/erlcloud?style=flat)](https://github.com/erlcloud/erlcloud/stargazers) - Cloud Computing library for Erlang (Amazon EC2, S3, SQS, SimpleDB, Mechanical Turk, ELB). ([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/erlcloud/)).
* [ex_aws](https://github.com/CargoSense/ex_aws) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CargoSense/ex_aws?style=flat)](https://github.com/CargoSense/ex_aws/stargazers) - AWS client, supporting Dynamo, Kinesis, Lambda, SQS, and S3.
* [ex_riak_cs](https://github.com/ayrat555/ex_riak_cs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ayrat555/ex_riak_cs?style=flat)](https://github.com/ayrat555/ex_riak_cs/stargazers) - Riak CS API client.
* [fleet_api](https://github.com/jordan0day/fleet-api) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jordan0day/fleet-api?style=flat)](https://github.com/jordan0day/fleet-api/stargazers) - A simple wrapper for the Fleet (CoreOS) API. Can be used with etcd tokens or via direct node URLs.
* [Gandi](https://github.com/Ahamtech/elixir-Gandi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ahamtech/elixir-Gandi?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ahamtech/elixir-Gandi/stargazers) - Gandi Wrapper for Leaseweb infrastructure.
* [IElixir](https://github.com/pprzetacznik/IElixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pprzetacznik/IElixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/pprzetacznik/IElixir/stargazers) - Jupyter's kernel for Elixir programming language.
* [k8s](https://github.com/coryodaniel/k8s) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coryodaniel/k8s?style=flat)](https://github.com/coryodaniel/k8s/stargazers) - Kubernetes Elixir client with CRD support, multi-cluster support, pluggable auth, and configurable middleware.
* [Kazan](https://github.com/obmarg/kazan) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/obmarg/kazan?style=flat)](https://github.com/obmarg/kazan/stargazers) - Kubernetes client for Elixir, generated from the k8s open API specifications.
* [Kubereq](https://github.com/mruoss/kubereq) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mruoss/kubereq?style=flat)](https://github.com/mruoss/kubereq/stargazers) - Kubernetes Client for Elixir based on Req.
* [Kubex](https://github.com/ingerslevio/kubex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ingerslevio/kubex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ingerslevio/kubex/stargazers) - Kubernetes client and integration for Elixir, written in pure Elixir.
* [Leaseweb](https://github.com/Ahamtech/elixir-leaseweb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Ahamtech/elixir-leaseweb?style=flat)](https://github.com/Ahamtech/elixir-leaseweb/stargazers) - Elixir Wrapper for Leaseweb infrastructure.
* [libcluster](https://github.com/bitwalker/libcluster) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bitwalker/libcluster?style=flat)](https://github.com/bitwalker/libcluster/stargazers) - Automatic cluster formation/healing for Elixir applications.([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/libcluster/readme.html)).
* [nodefinder](https://github.com/okeuday/nodefinder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/okeuday/nodefinder?style=flat)](https://github.com/okeuday/nodefinder/stargazers) - Strategies for automatic node discovery in Erlang.
* [nomad](https://github.com/sashaafm/nomad) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sashaafm/nomad?style=flat)](https://github.com/sashaafm/nomad/stargazers) - Create cloud portable Elixir and Phoenix apps. Write once, use everywhere.
* [sidejob](https://github.com/basho/sidejob) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/basho/sidejob?style=flat)](https://github.com/basho/sidejob/stargazers) - Parallel worker and capacity limiting library for Erlang.
* [sidetask](https://github.com/PSPDFKit-labs/sidetask) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/PSPDFKit-labs/sidetask?style=flat)](https://github.com/PSPDFKit-labs/sidetask/stargazers) - SideTask is an alternative to Task.Supervisor using Basho's sidejob library with parallelism and capacity limiting.
* [skycluster](https://github.com/Nebo15/skycluster) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nebo15/skycluster?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nebo15/skycluster/stargazers) - Automatic Erlang cluster formation, messaging and management for Elixir/Erlang applications. Integrated with Kubernetes.
* [vercel](https://github.com/Bounceapp/elixir-vercel) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Bounceapp/elixir-vercel?style=flat)](https://github.com/Bounceapp/elixir-vercel/stargazers) - An Elixir wrapper for Vercel's API.

## Code Analysis
*Libraries and tools for code base analysis, parsing, and manipulation.*

* [belvedere](https://github.com/nirvana/belvedere) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nirvana/belvedere?style=flat)](https://github.com/nirvana/belvedere/stargazers) - An example of CircleCI integration with Elixir.
* [coverex](https://github.com/alfert/coverex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alfert/coverex?style=flat)](https://github.com/alfert/coverex/stargazers) - Coverage Reports for Elixir.
* [credo](https://github.com/rrrene/credo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rrrene/credo?style=flat)](https://github.com/rrrene/credo/stargazers) - A static code analysis tool with a focus on code consistency and teaching Elixir. ([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/credo/Credo.html)).
* [DepViz](https://depviz.jasonaxelson.com/) - A visual tool to help developers understand Elixir recompilation in their projects. ([Code](https://github.com/axelson/dep_viz/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/axelson/dep_viz/?style=flat)](https://github.com/axelson/dep_viz//stargazers)).
* [dialyxir](https://github.com/jeremyjh/dialyxir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jeremyjh/dialyxir?style=flat)](https://github.com/jeremyjh/dialyxir/stargazers) - Mix tasks to simplify use of Dialyzer in Elixir projects.([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/dialyzex/Mix.Tasks.Dialyzer.html)).
* [ex_check](https://github.com/karolsluszniak/ex_check) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/karolsluszniak/ex_check?style=flat)](https://github.com/karolsluszniak/ex_check/stargazers) - One task to efficiently run all code analysis & testing tools in an Elixir project.
* [excellent_migrations](https://github.com/Artur-Sulej/excellent_migrations) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Artur-Sulej/excellent_migrations?style=flat)](https://github.com/Artur-Sulej/excellent_migrations/stargazers) - Detecting potentially dangerous operations in database migrations.
* [excoveralls](https://github.com/parroty/excoveralls) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/parroty/excoveralls?style=flat)](https://github.com/parroty/excoveralls/stargazers) - Coverage report tool for Elixir with coveralls.io integration.
* [exprof](https://github.com/parroty/exprof) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/parroty/exprof?style=flat)](https://github.com/parroty/exprof/stargazers) - A simple code profiler for Elixir, using eprof.
* [int_set](https://github.com/Cantido/int_set) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Cantido/int_set?style=flat)](https://github.com/Cantido/int_set/stargazers) - A time- and memory-efficient unordered data structure for positive integers.

## Command Line Applications
*Anything helpful for building CLI applications.*

* [elementtui](https://codeberg.org/edwinvanl/elementtui) - Library to help create terminal user interfaces (TUI).
* [ex_cli](https://github.com/tuvistavie/ex_cli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tuvistavie/ex_cli?style=flat)](https://github.com/tuvistavie/ex_cli/stargazers) - User friendly CLI apps for Elixir.
* [ex_prompt](https://github.com/behind-design/ex_prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/behind-design/ex_prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/behind-design/ex_prompt/stargazers) - Helper package to add interactivity to your command line applications as easy as possible.
* [firex](https://github.com/msoedov/firex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/msoedov/firex?style=flat)](https://github.com/msoedov/firex/stargazers) - Firex is a library for automatically generating command line interfaces (CLIs) from an elixir module.
* [getopt](https://github.com/jcomellas/getopt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jcomellas/getopt?style=flat)](https://github.com/jcomellas/getopt/stargazers) - Command-line options parser for Erlang.
* [loki](https://github.com/khusnetdinov/loki) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/khusnetdinov/loki?style=flat)](https://github.com/khusnetdinov/loki/stargazers) - Library for creating interactive command-line application.
* [optimus](https://github.com/savonarola/optimus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/savonarola/optimus?style=flat)](https://github.com/savonarola/optimus/stargazers) - Command-line option parser for Elixir inspired by [clap.rs](https://clap.rs/).
* [owl](https://github.com/fuelen/owl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fuelen/owl?style=flat)](https://github.com/fuelen/owl/stargazers) - Owl is a toolkit for writing command-line user interfaces in Elixir.
* [phoenix-cli](https://phoenix-cli.github.io/) - Command-line interface for Phoenix Framework like Rails commands.
* [progress_bar](https://github.com/henrik/progress_bar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/henrik/progress_bar?style=flat)](https://github.com/henrik/progress_bar/stargazers) - Command-line progress bars and spinners.
* [prompt](https://github.com/silbermm/prompt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/silbermm/prompt?style=flat)](https://github.com/silbermm/prompt/stargazers) - Toolkit for building command line applications in Elixir.
* [ratatouille](https://github.com/ndreynolds/ratatouille) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ndreynolds/ratatouille?style=flat)](https://github.com/ndreynolds/ratatouille/stargazers) - A TUI (terminal UI) kit for Elixir.
* [scribe](https://github.com/codedge-llc/scribe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/codedge-llc/scribe?style=flat)](https://github.com/codedge-llc/scribe/stargazers) - Pretty-print tables of Elixir structs and maps. Inspired by hirb.
* [table_rex](https://github.com/djm/table_rex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/djm/table_rex?style=flat)](https://github.com/djm/table_rex/stargazers) - Generate configurable ASCII style tables for display.
* [tabula](https://github.com/aerosol/tabula) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aerosol/tabula?style=flat)](https://github.com/aerosol/tabula/stargazers) - Pretty print list of Ecto query results / maps in ascii tables (GitHub Markdown/OrgMode).

## Configuration
*Libraries and tools working with configurations*

* [confex](https://github.com/Nebo15/confex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nebo15/confex?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nebo15/confex/stargazers) - Helper module that provides a nice way to read environment configuration at runtime.
* [configparser_ex](https://github.com/easco/configparser_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/easco/configparser_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/easco/configparser_ex/stargazers) - A simple Elixir parser for the same kind of files that Python's configparser library handles.
* [conform](https://github.com/bitwalker/conform) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bitwalker/conform?style=flat)](https://github.com/bitwalker/conform/stargazers) - Easy release configuration for Elixir apps.
* [dotenv](https://github.com/avdi/dotenv_elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/avdi/dotenv_elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/avdi/dotenv_elixir/stargazers) - A port of dotenv to Elixir.
* [enux](https://github.com/massivefermion/enux) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/massivefermion/enux?style=flat)](https://github.com/massivefermion/enux/stargazers) - utility package for loading, validating and documenting your app's configuration variables from env, json and jsonc files at runtime and injecting them into your environment.
* [figaro](https://github.com/trestrantham/ex_figaro) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trestrantham/ex_figaro?style=flat)](https://github.com/trestrantham/ex_figaro/stargazers) - Simple Elixir project configuration.
* [figaro_elixir](https://github.com/KamilLelonek/figaro-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KamilLelonek/figaro-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/KamilLelonek/figaro-elixir/stargazers) - Environmental variables manager for Elixir.
* [hush](https://github.com/gordalina/hush) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gordalina/hush?style=flat)](https://github.com/gordalina/hush/stargazers) - Read and inject configuration at runtime, and in release mode with support for multiple providers.
* [hush_aws_secrets_manager](https://github.com/gordalina/hush_aws_secrets_manager) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gordalina/hush_aws_secrets_manager?style=flat)](https://github.com/gordalina/hush_aws_secrets_manager/stargazers) - AWS Secrets Manager provider for hush.
* [hush_gcp_secret_manager](https://github.com/gordalina/hush_gcp_secret_manager) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gordalina/hush_gcp_secret_manager?style=flat)](https://github.com/gordalina/hush_gcp_secret_manager/stargazers) - Google Secret Manager provider for hush.
* [mahaul](https://github.com/emadalam/mahaul) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emadalam/mahaul?style=flat)](https://github.com/emadalam/mahaul/stargazers) - Supercharge your environment variables in Elixir. Parse and validate with compile time access guarantees, defaults, fallbacks and app pre-boot validations.
* [skogsra](https://github.com/gmtprime/skogsra) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gmtprime/skogsra?style=flat)](https://github.com/gmtprime/skogsra/stargazers) - Library to manage OS environment variables and application configuration options with ease.
* [sweetconfig](https://github.com/d0rc/sweetconfig) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/d0rc/sweetconfig?style=flat)](https://github.com/d0rc/sweetconfig/stargazers) - Read YAML configuration files from any point at your app.
* [weave](https://gitlab.com/gt8/open-source/elixir/weave) - JIT configuration loader that works with Kubernetes and Docker Swarm.

## Cryptography
*Encrypting and decrypting data*

* [aescmac](https://github.com/kleinernik/elixir-aes-cmac) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kleinernik/elixir-aes-cmac?style=flat)](https://github.com/kleinernik/elixir-aes-cmac/stargazers) - AES CMAC ([RFC 4493](https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc4493)) in Elixir.
* [cipher](https://github.com/rubencaro/cipher) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rubencaro/cipher?style=flat)](https://github.com/rubencaro/cipher/stargazers) - Elixir crypto library to encrypt/decrypt arbitrary binaries.
* [cloak](https://github.com/danielberkompas/cloak) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/danielberkompas/cloak?style=flat)](https://github.com/danielberkompas/cloak/stargazers) - Cloak makes it easy to use encryption with Ecto.([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/cloak/readme.html)).
* [comeonin](https://github.com/riverrun/comeonin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/riverrun/comeonin?style=flat)](https://github.com/riverrun/comeonin/stargazers) - Password hashing (argon2, bcrypt, pbkdf2_sha512) library for Elixir.([https://hexdocs.pm/comeonin/api-reference.html](https://hexdocs.pm/comeonin/api-reference.html)).
* [crypto_rsassa_pss](https://github.com/potatosalad/erlang-crypto_rsassa_pss) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/potatosalad/erlang-crypto_rsassa_pss?style=flat)](https://github.com/potatosalad/erlang-crypto_rsassa_pss/stargazers) - RSASSA-PSS Public Key Cryptographic Signature Algorithm for Erlang.
* [elixir_tea](https://github.com/keichan34/elixir_tea) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keichan34/elixir_tea?style=flat)](https://github.com/keichan34/elixir_tea/stargazers) - TEA implementation in Elixir.
* [ex_bcrypt](https://github.com/manelli/ex_bcrypt) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/manelli/ex_bcrypt?style=flat)](https://github.com/manelli/ex_bcrypt/stargazers) - Elixir wrapper for the OpenBSD bcrypt password hashing algorithm.
* [ex_crypto](https://github.com/ntrepid8/ex_crypto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ntrepid8/ex_crypto?style=flat)](https://github.com/ntrepid8/ex_crypto/stargazers) - Elixir wrapper for Erlang `crypto` and `public_key` modules. Provides sensible defaults for many crypto functions to make them easier to use.([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/ex_crypto/readme.html)).
* [exgpg](https://github.com/rozap/exgpg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rozap/exgpg?style=flat)](https://github.com/rozap/exgpg/stargazers) - Use gpg from Elixir.
* [nimble_totp](https://github.com/dashbitco/nimble_totp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dashbitco/nimble_totp?style=flat)](https://github.com/dashbitco/nimble_totp/stargazers) - Allows implementation of Time-based One-Time Passwords (TOTP) for 2FA.
* [ntru_elixir](https://github.com/alisinabh/ntru_elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alisinabh/ntru_elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/alisinabh/ntru_elixir/stargazers) - Elixir wrapper for libntru. A post quantum cryptography system.
* [pot](https://github.com/yuce/pot) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuce/pot?style=flat)](https://github.com/yuce/pot/stargazers) - Erlang library for generating one time passwords compatible with Google Authenticator.
* [rsa](https://github.com/trapped/elixir-rsa) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trapped/elixir-rsa?style=flat)](https://github.com/trapped/elixir-rsa/stargazers) - `public_key` cryptography wrapper for Elixir.
* [rsa_ex](https://github.com/anoskov/rsa-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/anoskov/rsa-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/anoskov/rsa-ex/stargazers) - Library for working with RSA keys.
* [siphash-elixir](https://github.com/whitfin/siphash-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/siphash-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/siphash-elixir/stargazers) - Elixir implementation of the SipHash hash family.
* [tea_crypto](https://github.com/keichan34/tea_crypto_erl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keichan34/tea_crypto_erl?style=flat)](https://github.com/keichan34/tea_crypto_erl/stargazers) - Tiny Encryption Algorithm implementation.

## CSV
*Libraries and implementations working with CSV.*

* [cesso](https://github.com/meh/cesso) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/cesso?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/cesso/stargazers) - CSV handling library for Elixir.
* [csv](https://github.com/beatrichartz/csv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/beatrichartz/csv?style=flat)](https://github.com/beatrichartz/csv/stargazers) - CSV Decoding and Encoding for Elixir.
* [csv2sql](https://github.com/Arp-G/csv2sql) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Arp-G/csv2sql?style=flat)](https://github.com/Arp-G/csv2sql/stargazers) - A fast and fully automated CSV to database importer.
* [csvlixir](https://github.com/jimm/csvlixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jimm/csvlixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/jimm/csvlixir/stargazers) - A CSV reading/writing application for Elixir.
* [ecsv](https://github.com/erpuno/ecsv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/erpuno/ecsv?style=flat)](https://github.com/erpuno/ecsv/stargazers) - Fast libcsv-based stream parser for Elixir.
* [nimble_csv](https://github.com/plataformatec/nimble_csv) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/plataformatec/nimble_csv?style=flat)](https://github.com/plataformatec/nimble_csv/stargazers) - A simple and fast CSV parsing and dumping library for Elixir.

## Data Visualization
*Libraries for creating visualizations with data.*

* [plox](https://github.com/gridpoint-com/plox) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gridpoint-com/plox?style=flat)](https://github.com/gridpoint-com/plox/stargazers) - Server-side rendered SVG graphing components for Phoenix and LiveView.
* [tucan](https://github.com/pnezis/tucan) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pnezis/tucan?style=flat)](https://github.com/pnezis/tucan/stargazers) - An Elixir plotting library on top of VegaLite.
* [vega_lite](https://github.com/livebook-dev/vega_lite) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/livebook-dev/vega_lite?style=flat)](https://github.com/livebook-dev/vega_lite/stargazers) - Elixir bindings for Vega-Lite.

## Date and Time
*Libraries for working with dates and times.*

* [block_timer](https://github.com/adamkittelson/block_timer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adamkittelson/block_timer?style=flat)](https://github.com/adamkittelson/block_timer/stargazers) - Macros to use :timer.apply_after and :timer.apply_interval with a block.
* [calendar](https://github.com/lau/calendar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lau/calendar?style=flat)](https://github.com/lau/calendar/stargazers) - Calendar is a date and time library for Elixir.
* [calendarific](https://github.com/Bounceapp/elixir-calendarific) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Bounceapp/elixir-calendarific?style=flat)](https://github.com/Bounceapp/elixir-calendarific/stargazers) - Calendarific is a wrapper for the holiday API Calendarific.
* [calixir](https://github.com/rengel-de/calixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rengel-de/calixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/rengel-de/calixir/stargazers) - Calixir is a port of the Lisp calendar software calendrica-4.0 to Elixir.
* [chronos](https://github.com/nurugger07/chronos) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nurugger07/chronos?style=flat)](https://github.com/nurugger07/chronos/stargazers) - An Elixir date/time library.
* [cocktail](https://github.com/peek-travel/cocktail) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/peek-travel/cocktail?style=flat)](https://github.com/peek-travel/cocktail/stargazers) - Elixir date recurrence library based on iCalendar events.
* [cronex](https://github.com/jbernardo95/cronex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jbernardo95/cronex?style=flat)](https://github.com/jbernardo95/cronex/stargazers) - Cron like system you can mount in your supervision tree.
* [crontab](https://github.com/jshmrtn/crontab) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jshmrtn/crontab?style=flat)](https://github.com/jshmrtn/crontab/stargazers) - A Cron Expressions Parser, Composer & Date Candidate Finder.
* [emojiclock](https://github.com/nathanhornby/emojiclock-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nathanhornby/emojiclock-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/nathanhornby/emojiclock-elixir/stargazers) - An Elixir module for giving you an emoji clock for a given hour.
* [ex_ical](https://github.com/fazibear/ex_ical) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fazibear/ex_ical?style=flat)](https://github.com/fazibear/ex_ical/stargazers) - ICalendar parser.
* [filtrex](https://github.com/rcdilorenzo/filtrex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rcdilorenzo/filtrex?style=flat)](https://github.com/rcdilorenzo/filtrex/stargazers) - A library for performing and validating complex SQL-like filters from a client (e.g. smart filters).
* [good_times](https://github.com/DevL/good_times) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DevL/good_times?style=flat)](https://github.com/DevL/good_times/stargazers) - Expressive and easy to use datetime functions.
* [jalaali](https://github.com/jalaali/elixir-jalaali) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jalaali/elixir-jalaali?style=flat)](https://github.com/jalaali/elixir-jalaali/stargazers) - Jalaali calendar implementation for Elixir.
* [milliseconds](https://github.com/davebryson/elixir_milliseconds) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/davebryson/elixir_milliseconds?style=flat)](https://github.com/davebryson/elixir_milliseconds/stargazers) - Simple library to work with milliseconds in Elixir.
* [moment](https://github.com/atabary/moment) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/atabary/moment?style=flat)](https://github.com/atabary/moment/stargazers) - Parse, validate, manipulate, and display dates in Elixir.
* [open_hours](https://github.com/hopsor/open_hours) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hopsor/open_hours?style=flat)](https://github.com/hopsor/open_hours/stargazers) - Time calculations using business hours.
* [quantum](https://github.com/quantum-elixir/quantum-core) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/quantum-elixir/quantum-core?style=flat)](https://github.com/quantum-elixir/quantum-core/stargazers) - Cron-like job scheduler for Elixir applications.
* [repeatex](https://github.com/rcdilorenzo/repeatex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rcdilorenzo/repeatex?style=flat)](https://github.com/rcdilorenzo/repeatex/stargazers) - Natural language parsing for repeating dates.

## Deployment
*Installing and running your code automatically on other machines.*

* [akd](https://github.com/annkissam/akd) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/annkissam/akd?style=flat)](https://github.com/annkissam/akd/stargazers) - Capistrano like, Configurable, and easy to set up Elixir Deployment Automation Framework.
* [ansible-elixir-stack](https://github.com/HashNuke/ansible-elixir-stack) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HashNuke/ansible-elixir-stack?style=flat)](https://github.com/HashNuke/ansible-elixir-stack/stargazers) - 1-command setup & deploys to servers, with first-class support for Phoenix apps.
* [bootleg](https://github.com/labzero/bootleg) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/labzero/bootleg?style=flat)](https://github.com/labzero/bootleg/stargazers) - Simple deployment and server automation for Elixir.
* [bottler](https://github.com/rubencaro/bottler) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rubencaro/bottler?style=flat)](https://github.com/rubencaro/bottler/stargazers) - Bottler is a collection of tools that aims to help you generate releases, ship them to your servers, install them there, and get them live on production.
* [edeliver](https://github.com/boldpoker/edeliver) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boldpoker/edeliver?style=flat)](https://github.com/boldpoker/edeliver/stargazers) - Deployment for Elixir and Erlang.
* [elixir-on-docker](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/elixir-on-docker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CrowdHailer/elixir-on-docker?style=flat)](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/elixir-on-docker/stargazers) - A project template to get started developing clustered Elixir applications for cloud environments.
* [exdm](https://github.com/joeyates/exdm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/joeyates/exdm?style=flat)](https://github.com/joeyates/exdm/stargazers) - Deploy Elixir applications via mix tasks.
* [exreleasy](https://github.com/miros/exreleasy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/miros/exreleasy?style=flat)](https://github.com/miros/exreleasy/stargazers) - Dead simple and Mix friendly tool for releasing Elixir applications.
* [gatling](https://github.com/hashrocket/gatling) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashrocket/gatling?style=flat)](https://github.com/hashrocket/gatling/stargazers) - Collection of mix tasks to automatically create a exrm release from git and launch/upgrade it on your server.
* [Gigalixir](https://www.gigalixir.com) - A fully-featured PaaS designed for Elixir. Supports clustering, hot upgrades, and remote console/observer. Free to try without a credit card.
* [heroku-buildpack-elixir](https://github.com/HashNuke/heroku-buildpack-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/HashNuke/heroku-buildpack-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/HashNuke/heroku-buildpack-elixir/stargazers) - Heroku buildpack to deploy Elixir apps to Heroku.

* [bamboo](https://github.com/thoughtbot/bamboo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thoughtbot/bamboo?style=flat)](https://github.com/thoughtbot/bamboo/stargazers) - Composable, testable and adapter based email library. Out of the box support for rendering with Phoenix and a plug for previewing sent emails in dev.

* [mailer](https://github.com/antp/mailer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/antp/mailer?style=flat)](https://github.com/antp/mailer/stargazers) - A simple SMTP mailer.
* [mailibex](https://github.com/awetzel/mailibex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awetzel/mailibex?style=flat)](https://github.com/awetzel/mailibex/stargazers) - Library containing Email-related implementations in Elixir: dkim, spf, dmark, mimemail, smtp.
* [mailman](https://github.com/kamilc/mailman) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kamilc/mailman?style=flat)](https://github.com/kamilc/mailman/stargazers) - Mailman provides a clean way of defining mailers in your Elixir applications.
* [pop3mail](https://hex.pm/packages/pop3mail) - Pop3 client to download email (including attachments) from the inbox via the commandline or Elixir API.
* [ravenx](https://github.com/acutario/ravenx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/acutario/ravenx?style=flat)](https://github.com/acutario/ravenx/stargazers) - Notification dispatch library for Elixir applications.
* [smoothie](https://github.com/jfrolich/smoothie) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jfrolich/smoothie?style=flat)](https://github.com/jfrolich/smoothie/stargazers) - Smoothie inline styles of your email templates, and generates a plain text version from the HTML.
* [swoosh](https://github.com/swoosh/swoosh) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swoosh/swoosh?style=flat)](https://github.com/swoosh/swoosh/stargazers) - Compose, deliver and test your Emails (with attachments!) easily in Elixir with adapters for SMTP, Sendgrid, Mandrill, Mailgun, Postmark and lots others, plus Phoenix integration with mailbox preview.

* [OK](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/OK) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CrowdHailer/OK?style=flat)](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/OK/stargazers) - Elegant error handling with result monads, featuring a simple & powerful `with` construct and a happy path pipe operator.
