## Eventhandling
*Sending/Emitting and receiving/handling Events in Elixir.*

* [cizen](https://gitlab.com/cizen/cizen) - Build highly concurrent, monitorable, and extensible applications with a collection of sagas.
* [event_bus](https://github.com/mustafaturan/event_bus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mustafaturan/event_bus?style=flat)](https://github.com/mustafaturan/event_bus/stargazers) - Simple event bus implementation with topic filtering and built-in event store and event watcher.
* [goldrush](https://github.com/DeadZen/goldrush) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DeadZen/goldrush?style=flat)](https://github.com/DeadZen/goldrush/stargazers) - Small, Fast event processing and monitoring for Erlang/OTP applications.
* [reaxive](https://github.com/alfert/reaxive) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alfert/reaxive?style=flat)](https://github.com/alfert/reaxive/stargazers) - Reaxive is a reactive event handling library, inspired by [Elm](http://elm-lang.org) and Reactive Extensions.
* [wait_for_it](https://github.com/jvoegele/wait_for_it) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jvoegele/wait_for_it?style=flat)](https://github.com/jvoegele/wait_for_it/stargazers) - Provides convenient and easy-to-use facilities for synchronizing concurrent activities.

## Examples and funny stuff
*Example code and stuff too funny or curious not to mention.*

* [butler_cage](https://github.com/keathley/butler_cage) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keathley/butler_cage?style=flat)](https://github.com/keathley/butler_cage/stargazers) - A Butler plugin for showing silly photos of Nick Cage.
* [butler_tableflip](https://github.com/keathley/butler_tableflip) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keathley/butler_tableflip?style=flat)](https://github.com/keathley/butler_tableflip/stargazers) - Flipping tables with butler.
* [changelog.com](https://github.com/thechangelog/changelog.com) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/thechangelog/changelog.com?style=flat)](https://github.com/thechangelog/changelog.com/stargazers) - CMS that runs changelog.com built with Phoenix 1.4.
* [coderplanets.com](https://github.com/coderplanets/coderplanets_server) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/coderplanets/coderplanets_server?style=flat)](https://github.com/coderplanets/coderplanets_server/stargazers) - GraphQL api for coderplanets.com built with Phoenix 1.4 and Absinthe.
* [dice](https://github.com/stocks29/dice) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stocks29/dice?style=flat)](https://github.com/stocks29/dice/stargazers) - Roll the dice, in Elixir.
* [elixir_koans](https://github.com/elixirkoans/elixir-koans) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixirkoans/elixir-koans?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixirkoans/elixir-koans/stargazers) - [Elixir koans](http://elixirkoans.io/) is a fun, easy way to get started with the elixir programming language.
* [ex_iss](https://github.com/cryptobird/ex_iss) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cryptobird/ex_iss?style=flat)](https://github.com/cryptobird/ex_iss/stargazers) - This package is for interfacing with the Open Notify API to information such as the ISS's current location, crew, and when it will pass over a location.
* [feedx](https://github.com/erneestoc/feedx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/erneestoc/feedx?style=flat)](https://github.com/erneestoc/feedx/stargazers) - Add social feed functionality to current applications. Exemplify OTP umbrella app, with 3 apps. Thin phoenix controllers.
* [harakiri](https://github.com/rubencaro/harakiri) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rubencaro/harakiri?style=flat)](https://github.com/rubencaro/harakiri/stargazers) - Help applications kill themselves.
* [hello_phoenix](https://github.com/bigardone/phoenix-react-redux-template) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bigardone/phoenix-react-redux-template?style=flat)](https://github.com/bigardone/phoenix-react-redux-template/stargazers) - Application template for SPAs with Phoenix, React and Redux.
* [hexpm](https://github.com/hexpm/hexpm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hexpm/hexpm?style=flat)](https://github.com/hexpm/hexpm/stargazers) - Source code for the hex package manager site built with Phoenix 1.3.
* [koans](https://github.com/dojo-toulouse/elixir-koans) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dojo-toulouse/elixir-koans?style=flat)](https://github.com/dojo-toulouse/elixir-koans/stargazers) - Learn Elixir by using elixir-koans.
* [lolcat](https://github.com/restartr/ex-lolcat) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/restartr/ex-lolcat?style=flat)](https://github.com/restartr/ex-lolcat/stargazers) - This is the clone of busyloop/lolcat. But it does not support animation and some features of the original.
* [magnetissimo](https://github.com/sergiotapia/magnetissimo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sergiotapia/magnetissimo?style=flat)](https://github.com/sergiotapia/magnetissimo/stargazers) - Web application that indexes all popular torrent sites, and saves it to the local database.
* [oop](https://github.com/wojtekmach/oop) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wojtekmach/oop?style=flat)](https://github.com/wojtekmach/oop/stargazers) - OOP in Elixir.
* [phoenix-chat-example](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-chat-example) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dwyl/phoenix-chat-example?style=flat)](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-chat-example/stargazers) - A step-by-step example/tutorial for building a Chat app in Phoenix for complete beginners. Covers testing, docs and deployment. Phoenix `1.5.3`.
* [phoenix-ecto-encryption-example](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-ecto-encryption-example) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dwyl/phoenix-ecto-encryption-example?style=flat)](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-ecto-encryption-example/stargazers) - A comprehensive example/tutorial showing people how to use Ecto Types to transparently encrypt/decrypt data in a Phoenix 1.4 app.
* [phoenix-flux-react](https://github.com/fxg42/phoenix-flux-react) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fxg42/phoenix-flux-react?style=flat)](https://github.com/fxg42/phoenix-flux-react/stargazers) - An experiment with Phoenix Channels, GenEvents, React and Flux.
* [phoenix-liveview-counter-tutorial](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-liveview-counter-tutorial) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dwyl/phoenix-liveview-counter-tutorial?style=flat)](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-liveview-counter-tutorial/stargazers) - complete beginners step-by-step tutorial building a real time counter in Phoenix `1.5.3` and LiveView `0.14.1`.
* [phoenix-todo-list-tutorial](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-todo-list-tutorial) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dwyl/phoenix-todo-list-tutorial?style=flat)](https://github.com/dwyl/phoenix-todo-list-tutorial/stargazers) - A complete beginners step-by-step tutorial for building a Todo List from scratch in Phoenix `1.5.3`.
* [real world example app](https://github.com/gothinkster/elixir-phoenix-realworld-example-app) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gothinkster/elixir-phoenix-realworld-example-app?style=flat)](https://github.com/gothinkster/elixir-phoenix-realworld-example-app/stargazers) - Elixir / Phoenix implementation of [RealWorld.io](https://realworld.io/) backend specs - a Medium clone.
* [rollex](https://gitlab.com/olhado/rollex) - Elixir library using a Pratt Parser algorithm to calculate dice rolls.
* [rubix](https://github.com/YellowApple/Rubix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/YellowApple/Rubix?style=flat)](https://github.com/YellowApple/Rubix/stargazers) - A very simple (and barely-functioning) Ruby runner for Elixir.
* [stranger](https://github.com/cazrin/stranger) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cazrin/stranger?style=flat)](https://github.com/cazrin/stranger/stargazers) - Elixir Phoenix app to chat anonymously with a randomly chosen stranger.
* [tilex](https://github.com/hashrocket/tilex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hashrocket/tilex?style=flat)](https://github.com/hashrocket/tilex/stargazers) - Source code for Hashrocket's TIL website built with Phoenix 1.3.
* [weather](https://github.com/tacticiankerala/elixir-weather) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tacticiankerala/elixir-weather?style=flat)](https://github.com/tacticiankerala/elixir-weather/stargazers) - A command line weather app built using Elixir.

## Feature Flags and Toggles
*Libraries to manage feature toggles (AKA feature flags): ON/OFF values that can be toggled at runtime through some interface*

* [ConfigCat](https://github.com/configcat/elixir-sdk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/configcat/elixir-sdk?style=flat)](https://github.com/configcat/elixir-sdk/stargazers) - Elixir SDK for ConfigCat hosted feature flag service.
* [flippant](https://github.com/sorentwo/flippant) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sorentwo/flippant?style=flat)](https://github.com/sorentwo/flippant/stargazers) - Feature flipping for the Elixir world.
* [fun_with_flags](https://github.com/tompave/fun_with_flags) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tompave/fun_with_flags?style=flat)](https://github.com/tompave/fun_with_flags/stargazers) - A feature toggle library using Redis or Ecto for persistence, an ETS cache for speed and PubSub for distributed cache busting. Comes with a management web UI for Phoenix and Plug.
* [molasses](https://github.com/securingsincity/molasses) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/securingsincity/molasses?style=flat)](https://github.com/securingsincity/molasses/stargazers) - A feature toggle library using redis or SQL (using Ecto) as a backing service.

## Feeds
*Libraries working with feeds like RSS or ATOM.*

* [atomex](https://github.com/Betree/atomex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Betree/atomex?style=flat)](https://github.com/Betree/atomex/stargazers) - ATOM feed builder with a focus on standards compliance, security and extensibility.
* [feeder](https://github.com/michaelnisi/feeder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/michaelnisi/feeder?style=flat)](https://github.com/michaelnisi/feeder/stargazers) - Parse RSS and Atom feeds.
* [feeder_ex](https://github.com/manukall/feeder_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/manukall/feeder_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/manukall/feeder_ex/stargazers) - RSS feed parser. Simple wrapper for feeder.
* [feedme](https://github.com/umurgdk/elixir-feedme) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/umurgdk/elixir-feedme?style=flat)](https://github.com/umurgdk/elixir-feedme/stargazers) - RSS/Atom parser built on erlang's xmerl xml parser.

## Files and Directories
*Libraries and implementations for working with files and directories.*

* [Belt](https://bitbucket.org/pentacent/belt/) - Extensible file upload library with support for SFTP, S3 and Filesystem storage.
* [dir_walker](https://github.com/pragdave/dir_walker) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pragdave/dir_walker?style=flat)](https://github.com/pragdave/dir_walker/stargazers) - DirWalker lazily traverses one or more directory trees, depth first, returning successive file names.
* [elixgrep](https://github.com/bbense/elixgrep) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bbense/elixgrep?style=flat)](https://github.com/bbense/elixgrep/stargazers) - A framework for doing Hadoop style Map/Reduce operations on collections of files.
* [ex_guard](https://github.com/slashmili/ex_guard) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slashmili/ex_guard?style=flat)](https://github.com/slashmili/ex_guard/stargazers) - ExGuard is a mix command to handle events on file system modifications.
* [ex_minimatch](https://github.com/gniquil/ex_minimatch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gniquil/ex_minimatch?style=flat)](https://github.com/gniquil/ex_minimatch/stargazers) - Globbing paths without walking the tree!.
* [exfile](https://github.com/keichan34/exfile) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keichan34/exfile?style=flat)](https://github.com/keichan34/exfile/stargazers) - File upload handling, persistence, and processing in Elixir and Plug.
* [exfswatch](https://github.com/falood/exfswatch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/falood/exfswatch?style=flat)](https://github.com/falood/exfswatch/stargazers) - A file change watcher wrapper based on __fs__.
* [eye_drops](https://github.com/rkotze/eye_drops) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rkotze/eye_drops?style=flat)](https://github.com/rkotze/eye_drops/stargazers) - Configurable mix task to watch file changes and run the corresponding command.
* [format_parser.ex](https://github.com/ahtung/format_parser.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ahtung/format_parser.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ahtung/format_parser.ex/stargazers) - Elixir library to figure out the type and the format of a file.
* [fs](https://github.com/synrc/fs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/synrc/fs?style=flat)](https://github.com/synrc/fs/stargazers) - Erlang FileSystem Listener.
* [fwatch](https://github.com/ryo33/fwatch-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ryo33/fwatch-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ryo33/fwatch-ex/stargazers) - A callback-based file watcher based on __fs__.
* [ivcu](https://github.com/elixir-ivcu/ivcu) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixir-ivcu/ivcu?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixir-ivcu/ivcu/stargazers) - File Validator, Converter, and Uploader.
* [librex](https://github.com/ricn/librex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ricn/librex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ricn/librex/stargazers) - Elixir library to convert office documents to other formats using LibreOffice.
* [Radpath](https://github.com/lowks/Radpath) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lowks/Radpath?style=flat)](https://github.com/lowks/Radpath/stargazers) - Path library for Elixir, inspired by Python's Enhpath.
* [sentix](https://github.com/whitfin/sentix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/sentix?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/sentix/stargazers) - A cross-platform file watcher for Elixir based on fswatch.
* [sizeable](https://github.com/arvidkahl/sizeable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/arvidkahl/sizeable?style=flat)](https://github.com/arvidkahl/sizeable/stargazers) - An Elixir library to make file sizes human-readable.
* [waffle](https://github.com/elixir-waffle/waffle) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixir-waffle/waffle?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixir-waffle/waffle/stargazers) - Flexible file upload and attachment library for Elixir.
* [zarex](https://github.com/ricn/zarex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ricn/zarex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ricn/zarex/stargazers) - Filename sanitization for Elixir.

## Forms
*Handling web forms and similar stuff.*

* [forms](https://github.com/spawnproc/forms) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spawnproc/forms?style=flat)](https://github.com/spawnproc/forms/stargazers) - Erlang Business Documents Generator.

## Framework Components
*Standalone component from web development frameworks.*

* [absinthe_plug](https://github.com/absinthe-graphql/absinthe_plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/absinthe-graphql/absinthe_plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/absinthe-graphql/absinthe_plug/stargazers) - Plug support for Absinthe.
* [access pass](https://github.com/AppDoctorIo/accesspass) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AppDoctorIo/accesspass?style=flat)](https://github.com/AppDoctorIo/accesspass/stargazers) - Authentication framework that can be used with or outside of phoenix. Similar to Addict but geared towards API usage.([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/access_pass/api-reference.html#content)).
* [addict](https://github.com/trenpixster/addict) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/trenpixster/addict?style=flat)](https://github.com/trenpixster/addict/stargazers) - User authentication for Phoenix Framework.
* [airbrake_plug](https://github.com/romul/airbrake_plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romul/airbrake_plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/romul/airbrake_plug/stargazers) - Report errors in your Plug stack or whatever to Airbrake.
* [Backpex](https://github.com/naymspace/backpex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/naymspace/backpex?style=flat)](https://github.com/naymspace/backpex/stargazers) - Highly customizable administration panel for Phoenix LiveView applications. ([Docs](https://hexdocs.pm/backpex/), [Demo](https://backpex.live/)).
* [better_params](https://github.com/sheharyarn/better_params) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sheharyarn/better_params?style=flat)](https://github.com/sheharyarn/better_params/stargazers) - Elixir Plug for cleaner request params in web apps.
* [blaguth](https://github.com/lexmag/blaguth) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/lexmag/blaguth?style=flat)](https://github.com/lexmag/blaguth/stargazers) - Basic Access Authentication in Plug applications.
* [commanded](https://github.com/slashdotdash/commanded) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slashdotdash/commanded?style=flat)](https://github.com/slashdotdash/commanded/stargazers) - Command handling middleware for Command Query Responsibility Segregation (CQRS) applications.
* [cors_plug](https://github.com/mschae/cors_plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mschae/cors_plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/mschae/cors_plug/stargazers) - An Elixir plug that adds CORS headers to requests and responds to preflight requests (OPTIONS).
* [corsica](https://github.com/whatyouhide/corsica) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whatyouhide/corsica?style=flat)](https://github.com/whatyouhide/corsica/stargazers) - Elixir library for dealing with CORS requests.
* [crudex](https://github.com/bitgamma/crudex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bitgamma/crudex?style=flat)](https://github.com/bitgamma/crudex/stargazers) - CRUD utilities for Phoenix and Ecto.
* [dayron](https://github.com/inaka/Dayron) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/inaka/Dayron?style=flat)](https://github.com/inaka/Dayron/stargazers) - A repository _similar_ to `Ecto.Repo` that works with REST API requests instead of a database.
* [ex_admin](https://github.com/smpallen99/ex_admin) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smpallen99/ex_admin?style=flat)](https://github.com/smpallen99/ex_admin/stargazers) - ExAdmin is an auto administration package for Elixir and the Phoenix Framework.
* [exdjango](https://github.com/nicksanders/exdjango) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nicksanders/exdjango?style=flat)](https://github.com/nicksanders/exdjango/stargazers) - A few elixir libraries for working with django.
* [exrecaptcha](https://github.com/adanselm/exrecaptcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adanselm/exrecaptcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/adanselm/exrecaptcha/stargazers) - Simple reCaptcha display/verify code for Elixir applications.
* [filterable](https://github.com/omohokcoj/filterable) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/omohokcoj/filterable?style=flat)](https://github.com/omohokcoj/filterable/stargazers) - Simple query params filtering for Phoenix framework inspired by Rails has_scope.
* [graphql_parser](https://github.com/graphql-elixir/graphql_parser) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/graphql-elixir/graphql_parser?style=flat)](https://github.com/graphql-elixir/graphql_parser/stargazers) - An Elixir binding for [libgraphqlparser](https://github.com/graphql/libgraphqlparser) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/graphql/libgraphqlparser?style=flat)](https://github.com/graphql/libgraphqlparser/stargazers).
* [http_router](https://github.com/sugar-framework/elixir-http-router) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sugar-framework/elixir-http-router?style=flat)](https://github.com/sugar-framework/elixir-http-router/stargazers) - HTTP Router with various macros to assist in developing your application and organizing your code.
* [kerosene](https://github.com/elixirdrops/kerosene) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixirdrops/kerosene?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixirdrops/kerosene/stargazers) - Pagination for Ecto and Phoenix.
* [live_vue](https://github.com/Valian/live_vue) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Valian/live_vue?style=flat)](https://github.com/Valian/live_vue/stargazers) - End-to-end reactivity for Phoenix LiveView and Vue.
* [mellon](https://github.com/sajmoon/mellon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sajmoon/mellon?style=flat)](https://github.com/sajmoon/mellon/stargazers) - An authentication module for Plug applications.
* [multiverse](https://github.com/Nebo15/multiverse) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Nebo15/multiverse?style=flat)](https://github.com/Nebo15/multiverse/stargazers) - Plug that allows to add version compatibility layers via API Request/Response Gateways.
* [params](https://github.com/vic/params) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/params?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/params/stargazers) - Use Ecto to enforce/validate parameters structure, akin to Rails' strong parameters.
* [phoenix_ecto](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix_ecto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/phoenixframework/phoenix_ecto?style=flat)](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix_ecto/stargazers) - Phoenix and Ecto integration.
* [phoenix_haml](https://github.com/chrismccord/phoenix_haml) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/chrismccord/phoenix_haml?style=flat)](https://github.com/chrismccord/phoenix_haml/stargazers) - Phoenix Template Engine for Haml.
* [phoenix_html](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix_html) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/phoenixframework/phoenix_html?style=flat)](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix_html/stargazers) - Phoenix.HTML functions for working with HTML strings and templates.
* [phoenix_html_sanitizer](https://github.com/elixirstatus/phoenix_html_sanitizer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixirstatus/phoenix_html_sanitizer?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixirstatus/phoenix_html_sanitizer/stargazers) - HTML Sanitizer integration for Phoenix.
* [phoenix_html_simplified_helpers](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/phoenix_html_simplified_helpers) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ikeikeikeike/phoenix_html_simplified_helpers?style=flat)](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/phoenix_html_simplified_helpers/stargazers) - Some helpers for phoenix html (truncate, time_ago_in_words, number_with_delimiter).

It looks abandoned: its last commit was on 2015 and its CI runs Elixir 1.0.3.

## Frameworks
*Web development frameworks.*

* [Ash Framework](https://github.com/ash-project/ash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ash-project/ash?style=flat)](https://github.com/ash-project/ash/stargazers) - A declarative, resource-oriented application framework for Elixir.
* [exelli](https://github.com/pigmej/exelli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pigmej/exelli?style=flat)](https://github.com/pigmej/exelli/stargazers) - An Elli Elixir wrapper with some sugar syntax goodies.
* [Flowbite](https://flowbite.com/docs/getting-started/phoenix/) - An open-source UI component library built with Tailwind CSS and compatible with Phoenix/Elixir.
* [Hologram](https://github.com/bartblast/hologram) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bartblast/hologram?style=flat)](https://github.com/bartblast/hologram/stargazers) - Full stack Elixir web framework that intelligently transpiles Elixir client-side code to JavaScript.
* [kitto](https://github.com/kittoframework/kitto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kittoframework/kitto?style=flat)](https://github.com/kittoframework/kitto/stargazers) - A framework for interactive dashboards.
* [n2o](https://github.com/synrc/n2o) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/synrc/n2o?style=flat)](https://github.com/synrc/n2o/stargazers) - Distributed Application Server.
* [nitro](https://github.com/synrc/nitro) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/synrc/nitro?style=flat)](https://github.com/synrc/nitro/stargazers) - Nitrogen-compatible Web Framework.
* [Petal Components](https://github.com/petalframework/petal_components) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/petalframework/petal_components?style=flat)](https://github.com/petalframework/petal_components/stargazers) - A set of HEEX components that makes it easy for Phoenix developers to build beautiful web apps.
* [phoenix](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/phoenixframework/phoenix?style=flat)](https://github.com/phoenixframework/phoenix/stargazers) - Elixir Web Framework targeting full-featured, fault tolerant applications with realtime functionality.
* [placid](https://github.com/slogsdon/placid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slogsdon/placid?style=flat)](https://github.com/slogsdon/placid/stargazers) - A REST toolkit for building highly-scalable and fault-tolerant HTTP APIs with Elixir.
* [rackla](https://github.com/AntonFagerberg/rackla) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AntonFagerberg/rackla?style=flat)](https://github.com/AntonFagerberg/rackla/stargazers) - API Gateways in Elixir.
* [relax](https://github.com/AgilionApps/relax) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AgilionApps/relax?style=flat)](https://github.com/AgilionApps/relax/stargazers) - Simple Elixir implementation of a [jsonapi.org](http://jsonapi.org) server.
* [rest](https://github.com/synrc/rest) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/synrc/rest?style=flat)](https://github.com/synrc/rest/stargazers) - Micro-REST framework with typed JSON.
* [RIG](https://github.com/Accenture/reactive-interaction-gateway) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Accenture/reactive-interaction-gateway?style=flat)](https://github.com/Accenture/reactive-interaction-gateway/stargazers) - Create low-latency, interactive user experiences for stateless microservices.

## Games
*Libraries for and implementations of games.*

* [Binbo](https://github.com/DOBRO/binbo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DOBRO/binbo?style=flat)](https://github.com/DOBRO/binbo/stargazers) - A chess representation written in Erlang using [Bitboards](https://www.chessprogramming.org/Bitboards), ready for use on game servers.
* [ECSx](https://hexdocs.pm/ecsx/initial_setup.html) - An Entity-Component-System framework providing a battle ship game as a tutorial ([read more on Dockyard blog](https://dockyard.com/blog/2023/07/06/ecsx-a-new-approach-to-game-development-in-elixir)).
* [entice](https://github.com/entice/entice) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/entice/entice?style=flat)](https://github.com/entice/entice/stargazers) - A distributed Entity-Component-System framework, providing its own example MMORPG server.
* [mines](https://github.com/kevlar1818/mines) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kevlar1818/mines?style=flat)](https://github.com/kevlar1818/mines/stargazers) - A minesweeper clone in the terminal.
* [pictionary](https://github.com/Arp-G/pictionary) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Arp-G/pictionary?style=flat)](https://github.com/Arp-G/pictionary/stargazers) - A multiplayer guessing and drawing game ([skribbl.io](https://skribbl.io/) clone).
* [rayex](https://github.com/shiryel/rayex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shiryel/rayex?style=flat)](https://github.com/shiryel/rayex/stargazers) - Raylib bindings to Elixir for games programming.
* [Rovex](https://github.com/emadb/rovex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/emadb/rovex?style=flat)](https://github.com/emadb/rovex/stargazers) - An implementation of the Mars Rover kata in Elixir transformed in a basic multiplayer game.
* [vim_snake](https://github.com/theanht1/vim_snake) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/theanht1/vim_snake?style=flat)](https://github.com/theanht1/vim_snake/stargazers) - A classical multiplayer snake game with Vim-style keybinding built with Phoenix framework.

## Geolocation
*Libraries for geocoding addresses and working with latitudes and longitudes.*

* [distance_api_matrix](https://github.com/C404/distance-matrix-api) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/C404/distance-matrix-api?style=flat)](https://github.com/C404/distance-matrix-api/stargazers) - Provide distance and heading calculations via Google distance matrix api.
* [geo](https://github.com/bryanjos/geo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bryanjos/geo?style=flat)](https://github.com/bryanjos/geo/stargazers) - A collection of GIS functions for Elixir.
* [geocalc](https://github.com/yltsrc/geocalc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yltsrc/geocalc?style=flat)](https://github.com/yltsrc/geocalc/stargazers) - Calculate distance, bearing and more between latitude/longitude points.
* [geocoder](https://github.com/knrz/geocoder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knrz/geocoder?style=flat)](https://github.com/knrz/geocoder/stargazers) - A simple, efficient geocoder/reverse geocoder with a built-in cache.
* [geohash](https://github.com/polmuz/elixir-geohash) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/polmuz/elixir-geohash?style=flat)](https://github.com/polmuz/elixir-geohash/stargazers) - Geohash encode/decode library.
* [geohash_nif](https://github.com/wstucco/geohash_nif/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wstucco/geohash_nif/?style=flat)](https://github.com/wstucco/geohash_nif//stargazers) - Drop in replacement for Geohash encode/decode library implemented as a NIF.
* [geohax](https://github.com/evuez/geohax) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/evuez/geohax?style=flat)](https://github.com/evuez/geohax/stargazers) - Geohash encoding and decoding with neighbors finder.
* [geoip](https://github.com/navinpeiris/geoip) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/navinpeiris/geoip?style=flat)](https://github.com/navinpeiris/geoip/stargazers) - Find geolocation for a given IP, hostname or `Plug.Conn`.
* [geolix](https://github.com/mneudert/geolix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mneudert/geolix?style=flat)](https://github.com/mneudert/geolix/stargazers) - MaxMind GeoIP2 database reader/decoder.
* [geonames](https://github.com/pareeohnos/geonames-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pareeohnos/geonames-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/pareeohnos/geonames-elixir/stargazers) - A simple Elixir wrapper around the GeoNames API.
* [ip2location](https://github.com/nazipov/ip2location-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nazipov/ip2location-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/nazipov/ip2location-elixir/stargazers) - An Elixir library for IP2Location database.
* [ipgeobase](https://github.com/sergey-chechaev/elixir_ipgeobase) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sergey-chechaev/elixir_ipgeobase?style=flat)](https://github.com/sergey-chechaev/elixir_ipgeobase/stargazers) - Find Russian and Ukraine city by IP address and find country for other country.
* [proj](https://github.com/CandyGumdrop/proj) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CandyGumdrop/proj?style=flat)](https://github.com/CandyGumdrop/proj/stargazers) - Elixir coordinate conversion library using OSGeo's PROJ.4.
* [segseg](https://github.com/pkinney/segseg_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkinney/segseg_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/pkinney/segseg_ex/stargazers) - Segment-segment intersection classifier and calculator.
* [srtm](https://github.com/adriankumpf/srtm) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/adriankumpf/srtm?style=flat)](https://github.com/adriankumpf/srtm/stargazers) - Query locations for elevation data from the NASA Shuttle Radar Topography Mission.
* [topo](https://github.com/pkinney/topo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkinney/topo?style=flat)](https://github.com/pkinney/topo/stargazers) - A Geometry library for Elixir that calculates spatial relationships between two geometries.
* [wheretz](https://github.com/UA3MQJ/wheretz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/UA3MQJ/wheretz?style=flat)](https://github.com/UA3MQJ/wheretz/stargazers) - Elixir version of Ruby gem for lookup of timezone by georgraphic coordinates.

## GUI
*Libraries for writing Graphical User Interfaces.*

* [scenic](https://github.com/boydm/scenic) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/boydm/scenic?style=flat)](https://github.com/boydm/scenic/stargazers) - Portable 2D UI framework.

## Hardware
*Hardware related things like I/O interfaces and such.*

* [elixir-circuits](https://github.com/elixir-circuits) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixir-circuits?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixir-circuits/stargazers) - Elixir access to hardware I/O interfaces such as GPIO, I2C, and SPI (old version [elixir_ale](https://github.com/fhunleth/elixir_ale) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fhunleth/elixir_ale?style=flat)](https://github.com/fhunleth/elixir_ale/stargazers)).
* [nerves](https://github.com/nerves-project/nerves) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nerves-project/nerves?style=flat)](https://github.com/nerves-project/nerves/stargazers) - Framework for building firmware for platforms like Raspberry Pi and BeagleBone Black.

## HTML
*Libraries and implementations working with HTML (for xml tools please go to the [XML](#xml) section).*

* [floki](https://github.com/philss/floki) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/philss/floki?style=flat)](https://github.com/philss/floki/stargazers) - A simple HTML parser that enables searching using CSS like selectors.
* [html_sanitize_ex](https://github.com/rrrene/html_sanitize_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rrrene/html_sanitize_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/rrrene/html_sanitize_ex/stargazers) - HTML sanitizer for Elixir.
* [meseeks](https://github.com/mischov/meeseeks#html) - A library for parsing and extracting data from HTML and XML with CSS or XPath selectors.
* [modest_ex](https://github.com/f34nk/modest_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f34nk/modest_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/f34nk/modest_ex/stargazers) - A library to do pipeable transformations on html strings with CSS selectors, e.g. find(), prepend(), append(), replace() etc.
* [myhtmlex](https://github.com/Overbryd/myhtmlex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Overbryd/myhtmlex?style=flat)](https://github.com/Overbryd/myhtmlex/stargazers) - Elixir/Erlang bindings for lexborisov's myhtml.
* [readability](https://github.com/keepcosmos/readability) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/keepcosmos/readability?style=flat)](https://github.com/keepcosmos/readability/stargazers) - Readability is for extracting and curating articles.
* [texas](https://gitlab.com/dgmcguire/texas) - Texas is a powerful abstraction over updating your clients using server-side rendering and server-side Virtual DOM diff/patching.
* [tidy_ex](https://github.com/f34nk/tidy_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/f34nk/tidy_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/f34nk/tidy_ex/stargazers) - Elixir binding to the granddaddy of HTML tools [http://www.html-tidy.org](http://www.html-tidy.org).
* [vnu-elixir](https://github.com/angelikatyborska/vnu-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/angelikatyborska/vnu-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/angelikatyborska/vnu-elixir/stargazers) - Elixir client for the [Nu HTML Checker](https://validator.w3.org/nu/). Provides HTML, CSS, and SVG validation.

## HTTP
*Libraries for working with HTTP and scraping websites.*

* [Ace](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/Ace) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CrowdHailer/Ace?style=flat)](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/Ace/stargazers) - HTTP web server and client, supports http1 and http2.
* [cauldron](https://github.com/meh/cauldron) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/cauldron?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/cauldron/stargazers) - An HTTP/SPDY server as a library.
* [Crawler](https://github.com/fredwu/crawler) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fredwu/crawler?style=flat)](https://github.com/fredwu/crawler/stargazers) - A high performance web crawler in Elixir.
* [Crawly](https://github.com/oltarasenko/crawly) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/oltarasenko/crawly?style=flat)](https://github.com/oltarasenko/crawly/stargazers) - high-level web crawling & scraping framework for Elixir.
* [elli](https://github.com/knutin/elli) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/knutin/elli?style=flat)](https://github.com/knutin/elli/stargazers) - Elli is a webserver you can run inside your Erlang application to expose an HTTP API.
* [etag_plug](https://github.com/sascha-wolf/etag_plug) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sascha-wolf/etag_plug?style=flat)](https://github.com/sascha-wolf/etag_plug/stargazers) - A simple to use shallow ETag plug.
* [explode](https://github.com/pkinney/explode) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pkinney/explode?style=flat)](https://github.com/pkinney/explode/stargazers) - An easy utility for responding with standard HTTP/JSON error payloads in Plug- and Phoenix-based applications.
* [exvcr](https://github.com/parroty/exvcr) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/parroty/exvcr?style=flat)](https://github.com/parroty/exvcr/stargazers) - HTTP request/response recording library for Elixir, inspired by VCR.
* [finch](https://github.com/sneako/finch) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sneako/finch?style=flat)](https://github.com/sneako/finch/stargazers) - An HTTP client with a focus on performance, built on top of Mint and NimblePool.
* [fuzzyurl](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gamache/fuzzyurl.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.ex/stargazers) - An Elixir library for parsing, constructing, and wildcard-matching URLs. Also available for [Ruby](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.rb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gamache/fuzzyurl.rb?style=flat)](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.rb/stargazers) and [JavaScript](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.js) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gamache/fuzzyurl.js?style=flat)](https://github.com/gamache/fuzzyurl.js/stargazers).
* [gun](https://github.com/ninenines/gun) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ninenines/gun?style=flat)](https://github.com/ninenines/gun/stargazers) - HTTP/1.1, HTTP/2 and Websocket client for Erlang/OTP.
* [hackney](https://github.com/benoitc/hackney) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benoitc/hackney?style=flat)](https://github.com/benoitc/hackney/stargazers) - Simple HTTP client written in Erlang.
* [http](https://github.com/slogsdon/http) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slogsdon/http?style=flat)](https://github.com/slogsdon/http/stargazers) - HTTP server for Elixir.
* [http_digex](https://github.com/techgaun/http_digex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/techgaun/http_digex?style=flat)](https://github.com/techgaun/http_digex/stargazers) - A module to create basic digest HTTP auth header.
* [http_proxy](https://github.com/KazuCocoa/http_proxy) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/KazuCocoa/http_proxy?style=flat)](https://github.com/KazuCocoa/http_proxy/stargazers) - Multi port HTTP Proxy.
* [httpoison](https://github.com/edgurgel/httpoison) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edgurgel/httpoison?style=flat)](https://github.com/edgurgel/httpoison/stargazers) - Yet Another HTTP client for Elixir powered by hackney.
* [httpotion](https://github.com/myfreeweb/httpotion) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/myfreeweb/httpotion?style=flat)](https://github.com/myfreeweb/httpotion/stargazers) - Fancy HTTP client for Elixir, based on ibrowse.
* [ivar](https://github.com/swelham/ivar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/swelham/ivar?style=flat)](https://github.com/swelham/ivar/stargazers) - A lightweight wrapper around HTTPoison that provides a fluent and composable way to build http requests.
* [lhttpc](https://github.com/talko/lhttpc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/talko/lhttpc?style=flat)](https://github.com/talko/lhttpc/stargazers) - A lightweight HTTP/1.1 client implemented in Erlang.
* [mint](https://github.com/ericmj/mint) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ericmj/mint?style=flat)](https://github.com/ericmj/mint/stargazers) - Functional HTTP client for Elixir with support for HTTP/1 and HTTP/2.
* [mnemonic_slugs](https://github.com/devshane/mnemonic_slugs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devshane/mnemonic_slugs?style=flat)](https://github.com/devshane/mnemonic_slugs/stargazers) - A memorable, mnemonic slug generator in Elixir.
* [mochiweb](https://github.com/mochi/mochiweb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mochi/mochiweb?style=flat)](https://github.com/mochi/mochiweb/stargazers) - MochiWeb is an Erlang library for building lightweight HTTP servers.

* [plug_wait1](https://github.com/wait1/plug_wait1) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/wait1/plug_wait1?style=flat)](https://github.com/wait1/plug_wait1/stargazers) - Plug adapter for the wait1 protocol.
* [raxx](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/raxx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/CrowdHailer/raxx?style=flat)](https://github.com/CrowdHailer/raxx/stargazers) - Interface for HTTP webservers, frameworks and clients.

* [river](https://github.com/peburrows/river) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/peburrows/river?style=flat)](https://github.com/peburrows/river/stargazers) - An HTTP/2 client that is lightweight and lightning fast.
* [scrape](https://github.com/Anonyfox/elixir-scrape) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Anonyfox/elixir-scrape?style=flat)](https://github.com/Anonyfox/elixir-scrape/stargazers) - Scrape any website, article or RSS/Atom Feed with ease.

* [SpiderMan](https://github.com/feng19/spider_man) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/feng19/spider_man?style=flat)](https://github.com/feng19/spider_man/stargazers) - A base-on Broadway fast high-level web crawling & scraping framework for Elixir.
* [tesla](https://github.com/teamon/tesla) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/teamon/tesla?style=flat)](https://github.com/teamon/tesla/stargazers) - HTTP client library, with support for middleware and multiple adapters.
* [Tube](https://github.com/narrowtux/Tube) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/narrowtux/Tube?style=flat)](https://github.com/narrowtux/Tube/stargazers) - Pure Elixir WebSocket client library.

* [webdriver](https://github.com/stuart/elixir-webdriver) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/stuart/elixir-webdriver?style=flat)](https://github.com/stuart/elixir-webdriver/stargazers) - This is an implementation of the WebDriver protocol client. It currently supports PhantomJS, FireFox, ChromeDriver and remote webdriver servers (e.g. Selenium).
* [yuri](https://github.com/kemonomachi/yuri) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kemonomachi/yuri?style=flat)](https://github.com/kemonomachi/yuri/stargazers) - Simple struct for representing URIs.

* [alchemic_avatar](https://github.com/zhangsoledad/alchemic_avatar) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zhangsoledad/alchemic_avatar?style=flat)](https://github.com/zhangsoledad/alchemic_avatar/stargazers) - Elixir library for generating letter avatar from string.

* [bump](https://github.com/evanfarrar/ex_bump) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/evanfarrar/ex_bump?style=flat)](https://github.com/evanfarrar/ex_bump/stargazers) - A BMP file writer in pure Elixir.

* [cloudex](https://github.com/smeevil/cloudex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/smeevil/cloudex?style=flat)](https://github.com/smeevil/cloudex/stargazers) - Cloudex is an Elixir library that can upload image files or urls to Cloudinary.
* [eikon](https://github.com/tchoutri/Eikon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/tchoutri/Eikon?style=flat)](https://github.com/tchoutri/Eikon/stargazers) - An Elixir library providing a read-only interface for image files.

* [ex_image_info](https://github.com/rNoz/ex_image_info) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rNoz/ex_image_info?style=flat)](https://github.com/rNoz/ex_image_info/stargazers) - An Elixir library to parse images (binaries) and get the dimensions, detected mime-type and overall validity for a set of image formats.
* [exexif](https://github.com/pragdave/exexif) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pragdave/exexif?style=flat)](https://github.com/pragdave/exexif/stargazers) - Pure Elixir library to extract TIFF and EFIX metadata from jpeg files.
* [exfavicon](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/exfavicon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ikeikeikeike/exfavicon?style=flat)](https://github.com/ikeikeikeike/exfavicon/stargazers) - An Elixir library for discovering favicons.
* [gi](https://github.com/LangPham/gi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/LangPham/gi?style=flat)](https://github.com/LangPham/gi/stargazers) - An Elixir wrapper for GraphicsMagick command line.
* [identicon](https://github.com/rbishop/identicon) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/rbishop/identicon?style=flat)](https://github.com/rbishop/identicon/stargazers) - An Elixir library for generating 5x5 identicons.
* [image64](https://hex.pm/packages/image64) - A tool for working with base64 encoded images.
* [imagineer](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/imagineer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/SenecaSystems/imagineer?style=flat)](https://github.com/SenecaSystems/imagineer/stargazers) - Image parsing in Elixir.
* [imgex](https://github.com/ianwalter/imgex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ianwalter/imgex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ianwalter/imgex/stargazers) - Unofficial client library for generating imgix URLs in Elixir.
* [mogrify](https://github.com/route/mogrify) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/route/mogrify?style=flat)](https://github.com/route/mogrify/stargazers) - An Elixir wrapper for ImageMagick command line.
* [png](https://github.com/yuce/png) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/yuce/png?style=flat)](https://github.com/yuce/png/stargazers) - A pure Erlang library for creating PNG images. It can currently create 8 and 16 bit RGB, RGB with alpha, indexed, grayscale and grayscale with alpha images.
* [thumbnex](https://github.com/talklittle/thumbnex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/talklittle/thumbnex?style=flat)](https://github.com/talklittle/thumbnex/stargazers) - Create thumbnails from images and video screenshots.
* [thumbor_client](https://github.com/globocom/thumbor-client-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/globocom/thumbor-client-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/globocom/thumbor-client-ex/stargazers) - Client for Thumbor.

## Instrumenting / Monitoring
*Libraries for collecting and exporting metrics.*

* [app_optex](https://github.com/sashman/app_optex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sashman/app_optex?style=flat)](https://github.com/sashman/app_optex/stargazers) - Client for AppOptics API. Send metrics and tags to AppOptics time series service.
* [appsignal-elixir](https://github.com/appsignal/appsignal-elixir/) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/appsignal/appsignal-elixir/?style=flat)](https://github.com/appsignal/appsignal-elixir//stargazers) - Collects error and performance data from your Elixir applications and sends it to [AppSignal](https://appsignal.com/).
* [elixometer](https://github.com/pinterest/elixometer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pinterest/elixometer?style=flat)](https://github.com/pinterest/elixometer/stargazers) - A light Elixir wrapper around exometer.
* [erlang-metrics](https://github.com/benoitc/erlang-metrics) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/benoitc/erlang-metrics?style=flat)](https://github.com/benoitc/erlang-metrics/stargazers) - A generic interface to different metrics systems in Erlang.
* [exometer](https://github.com/Feuerlabs/exometer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Feuerlabs/exometer?style=flat)](https://github.com/Feuerlabs/exometer/stargazers) - Basic measurement objects and probe behavior in Erlang.
* [folsom_ddb](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/folsom_ddb) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dalmatinerdb/folsom_ddb?style=flat)](https://github.com/dalmatinerdb/folsom_ddb/stargazers) - DalmatinerDB backend to store folsom metrics.
* [graphitex](https://github.com/msoedov/graphitex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/msoedov/graphitex?style=flat)](https://github.com/msoedov/graphitex/stargazers) - Graphite/Carbon client for Elixir.
* [instream](https://github.com/mneudert/instream) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mneudert/instream?style=flat)](https://github.com/mneudert/instream/stargazers) - InfluxDB driver for Elixir.
* [instrumental](https://github.com/undeadlabs/instrumental-ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/undeadlabs/instrumental-ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/undeadlabs/instrumental-ex/stargazers) - An Elixir client for [Instrumental](https://instrumentalapp.com/).
* [newrelic.ex](https://github.com/romul/newrelic.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/romul/newrelic.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/romul/newrelic.ex/stargazers) - Collects metrics from your Elixir/Phoenix application and sends them to [NewRelic](https://newrelic.com/).
* [prom_ex](https://github.com/akoutmos/prom_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/akoutmos/prom_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/akoutmos/prom_ex/stargazers) - Prometheus metrics and Grafana dashboards for all of your favorite Elixir libraries.
* [prometheus](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus.erl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus.erl?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus.erl/stargazers) - [Prometheus.io](https://prometheus.io) monitoring system and time series database client in Erlang.
* [prometheus-ecto](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-ecto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus-ecto?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-ecto/stargazers) - Ecto instrumenter for prometheus.ex.
* [prometheus-phoenix](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-phoenix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus-phoenix?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-phoenix/stargazers) - Phoenix instrumenter for prometheus.ex.
* [prometheus-plugs](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-plugs) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus-plugs?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus-plugs/stargazers) - Plugs instrumenters/exporter for prometheus.ex.
* [prometheus.ex](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus.ex/stargazers) - Elixir-friendly [Prometheus.io](https://prometheus.io) monitoring system and time series database client.
* [prometheus_process_collector](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus_process_collector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/deadtrickster/prometheus_process_collector?style=flat)](https://github.com/deadtrickster/prometheus_process_collector/stargazers) - Prometheus collector which exports the current state of process metrics including cpu, memory, file descriptor usage and native threads count as well as the process start and up times.
* [spandex](https://github.com/spandex-project/spandex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/spandex-project/spandex?style=flat)](https://github.com/spandex-project/spandex/stargazers) - Platform agnostic tracing library originally developed for Datadog APM.
* [telemetry](https://github.com/beam-telemetry/telemetry) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/beam-telemetry/telemetry?style=flat)](https://github.com/beam-telemetry/telemetry/stargazers) - Dynamic dispatching library for metrics and instrumentations.
* [wobserver](https://github.com/shinyscorpion/wobserver) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/shinyscorpion/wobserver?style=flat)](https://github.com/shinyscorpion/wobserver/stargazers) - Web based metrics, monitoring, and observer.

## JSON
*Libraries and implementations working with JSON.*

* [exjson](https://github.com/guedes/exjson) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/guedes/exjson?style=flat)](https://github.com/guedes/exjson/stargazers) - JSON parser and generator in Elixir.
* [ja_serializer](https://github.com/AgilionApps/ja_serializer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/AgilionApps/ja_serializer?style=flat)](https://github.com/AgilionApps/ja_serializer/stargazers) - JSONAPI.org Serialization in Elixir.
* [jason](https://github.com/michalmuskala/jason) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/michalmuskala/jason?style=flat)](https://github.com/michalmuskala/jason/stargazers) - A blazing fast JSON parser and generator in pure Elixir.
* [jazz](https://github.com/meh/jazz) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/jazz?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/jazz/stargazers) - Yet another library to handle JSON in Elixir.
* [joken](https://github.com/bryanjos/joken) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bryanjos/joken?style=flat)](https://github.com/bryanjos/joken/stargazers) - Encodes and decodes JSON Web Tokens.
* [jose](https://github.com/potatosalad/erlang-jose) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/potatosalad/erlang-jose?style=flat)](https://github.com/potatosalad/erlang-jose/stargazers) - JSON Object Signing and Encryption (JOSE) for Erlang and Elixir.
* [json](https://github.com/cblage/elixir-json) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cblage/elixir-json?style=flat)](https://github.com/cblage/elixir-json/stargazers) - Native JSON library for Elixir.
* [json_pointer](https://github.com/xavier/json_pointer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xavier/json_pointer?style=flat)](https://github.com/xavier/json_pointer/stargazers) - Implementation of RFC 6901 which defines a string syntax for identifying a specific value within a JSON document.
* [json_stream_encoder](https://github.com/TreyE/json_stream_encoder) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/TreyE/json_stream_encoder?style=flat)](https://github.com/TreyE/json_stream_encoder/stargazers) - JsonStreamEncoder is a streaming encoder for streaming JSON to an IOish thing in Elixir.
* [json_web_token_ex](https://github.com/garyf/json_web_token_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/garyf/json_web_token_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/garyf/json_web_token_ex/stargazers) - An Elixir implementation of the JSON Web Token (JWT) Standards Track (RFC 7519).
* [jsonapi](https://github.com/jeregrine/jsonapi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jeregrine/jsonapi?style=flat)](https://github.com/jeregrine/jsonapi/stargazers) - A project that will render your data models into [JSONAPI Documents](http://jsonapi.org/format/).
* [jsonc](https://github.com/massivefermion/jsonc) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/massivefermion/jsonc?style=flat)](https://github.com/massivefermion/jsonc/stargazers) - Utilities for working with [jsonc](https://komkom.github.io/jsonc-playground), a superset of json.
* [jsx](https://github.com/talentdeficit/jsx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/talentdeficit/jsx?style=flat)](https://github.com/talentdeficit/jsx/stargazers) - An Erlang application for consuming, producing, and manipulating json.
* [jwalk](https://github.com/jr0senblum/jwalk) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jr0senblum/jwalk?style=flat)](https://github.com/jr0senblum/jwalk/stargazers) - Helper module for working with Erlang representations of JSON.
* [jwtex](https://github.com/mschae/jwtex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mschae/jwtex?style=flat)](https://github.com/mschae/jwtex/stargazers) - A library to encode and decode [JWT tokens](http://jwt.io/).
* [poison](https://github.com/devinus/poison) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devinus/poison?style=flat)](https://github.com/devinus/poison/stargazers) - Poison is a new JSON library for Elixir focusing on wicked-fast speed without sacrificing simplicity, completeness, or correctness.
* [tiny](https://github.com/whitfin/tiny) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/tiny?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/tiny/stargazers) - Tiny, fast and fully compliant JSON parser for Elixir.
* [world_json](https://github.com/camshaft/world_json_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camshaft/world_json_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/camshaft/world_json_ex/stargazers) - topojson country and state/province collections for elixir/erlang.

## Languages

## Macros
*Macros for faster and easier development. Sugar for your code.*

* [anaphora](https://github.com/sviridov/anaphora-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/sviridov/anaphora-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/sviridov/anaphora-elixir/stargazers) - Anaphora is the anaphoric macro collection for Elixir. An anaphoric macro is one that deliberately captures a variable (typically it) from forms supplied to the macro.
* [apix](https://github.com/liveforeverx/apix) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/liveforeverx/apix?style=flat)](https://github.com/liveforeverx/apix/stargazers) - Simple convention and DSL for transformation of elixir functions to an API for later documentation and or validation.
* [backports](https://github.com/leifg/backports) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leifg/backports?style=flat)](https://github.com/leifg/backports/stargazers) - Use new functions in Elixir 1.1 and 1.2.
* [crudry](https://github.com/gabrielpra1/crudry) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gabrielpra1/crudry?style=flat)](https://github.com/gabrielpra1/crudry/stargazers) - Crudry is an elixir library for DRYing CRUD of Phoenix Contexts and Absinthe Resolvers.
* [eventsourced](https://github.com/slashdotdash/eventsourced) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slashdotdash/eventsourced?style=flat)](https://github.com/slashdotdash/eventsourced/stargazers) - Build functional, event-sourced domain models.
* [expat](https://github.com/vic/expat) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/expat?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/expat/stargazers) - Reusable, composable patterns across Elixir libraries.
* [guardsafe](https://github.com/DevL/guardsafe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/DevL/guardsafe?style=flat)](https://github.com/DevL/guardsafe/stargazers) - Macros expanding into code that can be safely used in guard clauses.
* [kwfuns](https://github.com/RobertDober/lab42_defkw) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/RobertDober/lab42_defkw?style=flat)](https://github.com/RobertDober/lab42_defkw/stargazers) - Macros to create functions with syntax based keyword parameters with default values.
* [lineo](https://github.com/camshaft/lineo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camshaft/lineo?style=flat)](https://github.com/camshaft/lineo/stargazers) - parse transform for accurate line numbers.
* [matcha](https://github.com/christhekeele/matcha) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/christhekeele/matcha?style=flat)](https://github.com/christhekeele/matcha/stargazers) - First-class match specifications for Elixir `:ets` querying and function call tracing.
* [mdef](https://github.com/pragdave/mdef) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pragdave/mdef?style=flat)](https://github.com/pragdave/mdef/stargazers) - Easily define multiple function heads in Elixir.
* [named_args](https://github.com/mgwidmann/named_args) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mgwidmann/named_args?style=flat)](https://github.com/mgwidmann/named_args/stargazers) - Allows named arg style arguments in Elixir.
* [ok_jose](https://github.com/vic/ok_jose) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/ok_jose?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/ok_jose/stargazers) - Pipe elixir functions that match `{:ok,_}`, `{:error,_}` tuples or custom patterns.
* [opus](https://github.com/zorbash/opus) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zorbash/opus?style=flat)](https://github.com/zorbash/opus/stargazers) - A framework for pluggable business logic components.
* [pathex](https://github.com/hissssst/pathex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hissssst/pathex?style=flat)](https://github.com/hissssst/pathex/stargazers) - Zero-dependency, blazing fast functional lenses.
* [pattern_tap](https://github.com/mgwidmann/elixir-pattern_tap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/mgwidmann/elixir-pattern_tap?style=flat)](https://github.com/mgwidmann/elixir-pattern_tap/stargazers) - Macro for tapping into a pattern match while using the pipe operator.
* [pipe_here](https://github.com/vic/pipe_here) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/pipe_here?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/pipe_here/stargazers) - Easily pipe values into any argument position.
* [pipes](https://github.com/batate/elixir-pipes) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/batate/elixir-pipes?style=flat)](https://github.com/batate/elixir-pipes/stargazers) - Macros for more flexible composition with the Elixir Pipe operator.
* [pit](https://github.com/vic/pit) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/vic/pit?style=flat)](https://github.com/vic/pit/stargazers) - Transform values as they flow inside a pipe.
* [rebind](https://github.com/camshaft/rebind) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/camshaft/rebind?style=flat)](https://github.com/camshaft/rebind/stargazers) - rebind parse transform for Erlang.
* [rulex](https://github.com/awetzel/rulex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awetzel/rulex?style=flat)](https://github.com/awetzel/rulex/stargazers) - Simple rule handler using Elixir pattern matching.
* [shorter_maps](https://github.com/meyercm/shorter_maps) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meyercm/shorter_maps?style=flat)](https://github.com/meyercm/shorter_maps/stargazers) - ~M sigil for map shorthand. `~M{id name} ~> %{id: id, name: name}`.
* [then](https://github.com/bardoor/then) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bardoor/then?style=flat)](https://github.com/bardoor/then/stargazers) - Simple way to set after-function callback.
* [typed_struct](https://github.com/ejpcmac/typed_struct) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ejpcmac/typed_struct?style=flat)](https://github.com/ejpcmac/typed_struct/stargazers) - An Elixir library for defining structs with a type without writing boilerplate code.
* [typed_structor](https://github.com/elixir-typed-structor/typed_structor) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixir-typed-structor/typed_structor?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixir-typed-structor/typed_structor/stargazers) - A library for defining structs with types effortlessly.
* [unsafe](https://github.com/whitfin/unsafe) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/whitfin/unsafe?style=flat)](https://github.com/whitfin/unsafe/stargazers) - Generate easy unsafe (!) bindings for Elixir functions.

## Markdown
*Libraries and tools working with Markdown and such.*

* [cmark](https://github.com/asaaki/cmark.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asaaki/cmark.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/asaaki/cmark.ex/stargazers) - Elixir NIF for CommonMark (in C), a parser following the CommonMark spec.
* [discount](https://github.com/asaaki/discount.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asaaki/discount.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/asaaki/discount.ex/stargazers) - Elixir NIF for discount, a Markdown parser.
* [earmark](https://github.com/pragdave/earmark) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pragdave/earmark?style=flat)](https://github.com/pragdave/earmark/stargazers) - Markdown parser for Elixir.
* [Markdown](https://github.com/devinus/markdown) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/devinus/markdown?style=flat)](https://github.com/devinus/markdown/stargazers) - Implemented entirely as a NIF binding to the Hoedown library.
* [Pandex](https://github.com/filterkaapi/pandex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/filterkaapi/pandex?style=flat)](https://github.com/filterkaapi/pandex/stargazers) - Lightweight Elixir wrapper for Pandoc. Converts Markdown, CommonMark, HTML, Latex, HTML, HTML5, opendocument, rtf, texttile, asciidoc to each other.

## Networking
*Libraries and tools for using network related stuff.*

* [asn](https://github.com/ephe-meral/asn) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ephe-meral/asn?style=flat)](https://github.com/ephe-meral/asn/stargazers) - Can be used to map from IP to AS to ASN.
* [chatter](https://github.com/dbeck/chatter_ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dbeck/chatter_ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/dbeck/chatter_ex/stargazers) - Secure message broadcasting based on a mixture of UDP multicast and TCP.
* [download](https://github.com/asiniy/download) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/asiniy/download?style=flat)](https://github.com/asiniy/download/stargazers) - Download files from the internet easily.
* [eio](https://github.com/falood/eio) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/falood/eio?style=flat)](https://github.com/falood/eio/stargazers) - Elixir server of engine.io.
* [ExPcap](https://github.com/cobenian/expcap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cobenian/expcap?style=flat)](https://github.com/cobenian/expcap/stargazers) - PCAP parser written in Elixir.
* [Firezone](https://github.com/firezone/firezone) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/firezone/firezone?style=flat)](https://github.com/firezone/firezone/stargazers) - Open-source VPN server and egress firewall for Linux built on WireGuard. Firezone is easy to set up (all dependencies are bundled thanks to Chef Omnibus), secure, performant, and self hostable.
* [FlyingDdns](https://gitlab.com/timopallach/FlyingDdns) - A dyndns server written in elixir.
* [hades](https://github.com/fklement/hades) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fklement/hades?style=flat)](https://github.com/fklement/hades/stargazers) - A wrapper for NMAP written in Elixir.
* [mac](https://github.com/ephe-meral/mac) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ephe-meral/mac?style=flat)](https://github.com/ephe-meral/mac/stargazers) - Can be used to find a vendor of a MAC given in hexadecimal string (according to IEEE).
* [pool](https://github.com/slogsdon/pool) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/slogsdon/pool?style=flat)](https://github.com/slogsdon/pool/stargazers) - Socket acceptor pool for Elixir.
* [reagent](https://github.com/meh/reagent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/reagent?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/reagent/stargazers) - reagent is a socket acceptor pool for Elixir.
* [sise](https://github.com/aytchell/sise) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/aytchell/sise?style=flat)](https://github.com/aytchell/sise/stargazers) - A simple to use SSDP client.
* [sockerl](https://github.com/Pouriya-Jahanbakhsh/sockerl) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/Pouriya-Jahanbakhsh/sockerl?style=flat)](https://github.com/Pouriya-Jahanbakhsh/sockerl/stargazers) - Sockerl is an advanced Erlang/Elixir socket library for TCP protocols and provides fast, useful and easy-to-use API for implementing servers, clients and client connection pools.
* [socket](https://github.com/meh/elixir-socket) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/elixir-socket?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/elixir-socket/stargazers) - Socket wrapping for Elixir.
* [sshkit](https://github.com/bitcrowd/sshkit.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bitcrowd/sshkit.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/bitcrowd/sshkit.ex/stargazers) - An Elixir toolkit for performing tasks on one or more servers, built on top of Erlang’s SSH application.
* [torex](https://github.com/alexfilatov/torex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/alexfilatov/torex?style=flat)](https://github.com/alexfilatov/torex/stargazers) - Simple Tor connection library.

* [wifi](https://github.com/gausby/wifi) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/gausby/wifi?style=flat)](https://github.com/gausby/wifi/stargazers) - Various utility functions for working with the local Wifi network in Elixir.
* [wpa_supplicant](https://github.com/fhunleth/wpa_supplicant.ex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/fhunleth/wpa_supplicant.ex?style=flat)](https://github.com/fhunleth/wpa_supplicant.ex/stargazers) - Elixir interface to the wpa_supplicant.

## Office
*Libraries for working with office suite documents.*

* [elixlsx](https://github.com/xou/elixlsx) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/xou/elixlsx?style=flat)](https://github.com/xou/elixlsx/stargazers) - A writer for XLSX files.
* [excellent](https://github.com/leifg/excellent) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/leifg/excellent?style=flat)](https://github.com/leifg/excellent/stargazers) - An OpenXL (Excel 2000) Parser for Elixir.
* [xlsxir](https://github.com/kennellroxco/xlsxir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/kennellroxco/xlsxir?style=flat)](https://github.com/kennellroxco/xlsxir/stargazers) - Xlsx file parser with support for ISO 8601 date formats. Data is extracted to an Erlang Term Storage (ETS) table and is accessed through various functions.

* [redo](https://github.com/heroku/redo) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/heroku/redo?style=flat)](https://github.com/heroku/redo/stargazers) - Heroku's pipelining redis client for erlang.
* [rethinkdb](https://github.com/hamiltop/rethinkdb-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/hamiltop/rethinkdb-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/hamiltop/rethinkdb-elixir/stargazers) - Rethinkdb client in pure Elixir using JSON protocol.

* [shards](https://github.com/cabol/shards) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/cabol/shards?style=flat)](https://github.com/cabol/shards/stargazers) - Transparent and out-of-box Sharding support for Erlang/Elixir ETS tables.
* [sql_dust](https://github.com/bettyblocks/sql_dust) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/bettyblocks/sql_dust?style=flat)](https://github.com/bettyblocks/sql_dust/stargazers) - Generate (complex) SQL queries using magical Elixir SQL dust.

* [tds](https://github.com/livehelpnow/tds) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/livehelpnow/tds?style=flat)](https://github.com/livehelpnow/tds/stargazers) - MSSQL / TDS Database driver for Elixir.
* [tds_ecto](https://github.com/livehelpnow/tds_ecto) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/livehelpnow/tds_ecto?style=flat)](https://github.com/livehelpnow/tds_ecto/stargazers) - MSSQL / TDS Adapter for Ecto.

* [triplex](https://github.com/ateliware/triplex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ateliware/triplex?style=flat)](https://github.com/ateliware/triplex/stargazers) - Database multitenancy with postgres schemas for Elixir applications.

## Queue

* [adap](https://github.com/awetzel/adap) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/awetzel/adap?style=flat)](https://github.com/awetzel/adap/stargazers) - Create a data stream across your information systems to query, augment and transform data according to Elixir matching rules.
* [amqp](https://github.com/pma/amqp) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/pma/amqp?style=flat)](https://github.com/pma/amqp/stargazers) - Simple Elixir wrapper for the Erlang RabbitMQ client, based on Langohr.
* [broadway](https://github.com/dashbitco/broadway) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/dashbitco/broadway?style=flat)](https://github.com/dashbitco/broadway/stargazers) - Concurrent and multi-stage data ingestion and data processing with Elixir.

* [cspex](https://github.com/costaraphael/cspex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/costaraphael/cspex?style=flat)](https://github.com/costaraphael/cspex/stargazers) - Simple, OTP compliant, Elixir implementation of CSP channels.

* [signaturex](https://github.com/edgurgel/signaturex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/edgurgel/signaturex?style=flat)](https://github.com/edgurgel/signaturex/stargazers) - Simple key/secret based authentication for APIs.

* [urna](https://github.com/meh/urna) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meh/urna?style=flat)](https://github.com/meh/urna/stargazers) - Urna is a simple DSL around cauldron to implement REST services.

The decoder will return the checksum value of the info dictionary, if an info dictionary was found in the input.

* [tau](https://github.com/FranklinChen/tau) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/FranklinChen/tau?style=flat)](https://github.com/FranklinChen/tau/stargazers) - Provide the famous mathematical constant, tau, τ = 6.2831....
* [tomlex](https://github.com/zamith/tomlex) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zamith/tomlex?style=flat)](https://github.com/zamith/tomlex/stargazers) - A TOML parser for Elixir.
* [transformer](https://github.com/ByeongUkChoi/transformer) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/ByeongUkChoi/transformer?style=flat)](https://github.com/ByeongUkChoi/transformer/stargazers) - Flexible type conversion lightweight library.
* [ua_inspector](https://github.com/elixytics/ua_inspector) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/elixytics/ua_inspector?style=flat)](https://github.com/elixytics/ua_inspector/stargazers) - User agent parser library like `piwik/device-detector`.
* [ua_parser2](https://github.com/nazipov/ua_parser2-elixir) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/nazipov/ua_parser2-elixir?style=flat)](https://github.com/nazipov/ua_parser2-elixir/stargazers) - A port of ua-parser2 to Elixir. User agent parser library.
* [unique_names_generator](https://github.com/jongirard/unique_names_generator) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/jongirard/unique_names_generator?style=flat)](https://github.com/jongirard/unique_names_generator/stargazers) - Generate seeded random and unique names.
* [unit_fun](https://github.com/meadsteve/unit_fun) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/meadsteve/unit_fun?style=flat)](https://github.com/meadsteve/unit_fun/stargazers) - Attempt to add units to numbers in elixir to give some added type safety when dealing with numeric quantities.
* [uuid](https://github.com/zyro/elixir-uuid) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/zyro/elixir-uuid?style=flat)](https://github.com/zyro/elixir-uuid/stargazers) - UUID generator and utilities for Elixir.

* [veritaserum](https://github.com/uesteibar/veritaserum) [![GitHub stars](https://img.shields.io/github/stars/uesteibar/veritaserum?style=flat)](https://github.com/uesteibar/veritaserum/stargazers) - Sentiment analysis based on afinn-165, emojis and some enhancements.
